\section{Priority Full-Text Sources}



\section{Dominium / Domino}

\vonecallout{DomSlate}{Source}{\texttt{current} \texttt{human\_\allowbreak{}full\_\allowbreak{}text} \texttt{current\_\allowbreak{}repo\_\allowbreak{}truth} Source: \texttt{README.\allowbreak{}md}.\allowbreak{} Reason: required high-\allowbreak{}authority orientation source.\allowbreak{}}

\subsection{Dominium / Domino}

Dominium is a deterministic, contract-\allowbreak{}governed simulation game and operating

environment built on the Domino deterministic substrate.\allowbreak{}


The project is about invention, production, logistics, economics, settlement,

trust, communication, and institutional power emerging from lawful simulation

rather than scripted outcomes.\allowbreak{} Commands, processes, packs, capabilities,

diagnostics, evidence, and replay proof are first-\allowbreak{}class surfaces.\allowbreak{} Invalid action

must refuse explicitly; hidden fallback behavior is not part of the model.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{Home Point}

Use this README as the project home point.\allowbreak{} It orients the product, repository,

and common proof commands.\allowbreak{} It is not the highest authority.\allowbreak{}


Authority starts here:


\begin{itemize}
\item Canon: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}canon/\allowbreak{}constitution\_\allowbreak{}v1.\allowbreak{}md}
\item Glossary: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}canon/\allowbreak{}glossary\_\allowbreak{}v1.\allowbreak{}md}
\item Agent governance: \texttt{AGENTS.\allowbreak{}md}
\item Canon index: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}CANON\_\allowbreak{}INDEX.\allowbreak{}md}
\item Current queue: \texttt{.\allowbreak{}aide/\allowbreak{}queue/\allowbreak{}current.\allowbreak{}toml}
\item Foundation status: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}repo/\allowbreak{}FOUNDATION\_\allowbreak{}LOCK.\allowbreak{}md}
\item Build guide: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}development/\allowbreak{}guides/\allowbreak{}BUILDING.\allowbreak{}md}
\item Test tiers: \texttt{contracts/\allowbreak{}testing/\allowbreak{}test\_\allowbreak{}tiers.\allowbreak{}contract.\allowbreak{}toml}
\item Public surface registry: \texttt{contracts/\allowbreak{}public\_\allowbreak{}surface/\allowbreak{}public\_\allowbreak{}surface.\allowbreak{}contract.\allowbreak{}toml}
\end{itemize}

Repo artifacts outrank chat memory, generated echoes, convenience summaries, and

old planning notes.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{Current State}

Current committed program position:


\begin{itemize}
\item Foundation Lock: \texttt{PASS\_\allowbreak{}WITH\_\allowbreak{}WARNINGS}.\allowbreak{}
\item Post-\allowbreak{}wave queue state: \texttt{post\_\allowbreak{}wave\_\allowbreak{}1\_\allowbreak{}pass\_\allowbreak{}with\_\allowbreak{}warnings}.\allowbreak{}
\item Completed narrow Workbench validation slice:
\end{itemize}
\texttt{WORKBENCH-\allowbreak{}VALIDATION-\allowbreak{}SLICE-\allowbreak{}01}.\allowbreak{}

\begin{itemize}
\item Current next task: \texttt{COMMAND-\allowbreak{}RESULT-\allowbreak{}VIEW-\allowbreak{}SLICE-\allowbreak{}01}.\allowbreak{}
\item Alternate next task: \texttt{PACKAGE-\allowbreak{}MOUNT-\allowbreak{}SLICE-\allowbreak{}01}.\allowbreak{}
\item Secondary follow-\allowbreak{}up: \texttt{POINTER-\allowbreak{}WIDTH-\allowbreak{}SERIALIZATION-\allowbreak{}AUDIT-\allowbreak{}01}.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

The current queue does not authorize broad feature work.\allowbreak{} Broad Workbench UI,

runtime module loading, provider runtime, package runtime, gameplay, renderer

implementation, native GUI, and release publication remain blocked until later

reviewed phases explicitly open them.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{What This Is}

Domino is the reusable deterministic substrate: execution, ordering, storage,

replay, ABI-\allowbreak{}facing boundaries, and other engine mechanisms.\allowbreak{}


Dominium is the official game, product, and domain layer on top of Domino.\allowbreak{} It

defines rules, process meaning, law targets, domain interpretation, authored

content use, and product composition.\allowbreak{}


Workbench is the richest operator environment for validation, evidence,

inspection, and later editing workflows.\allowbreak{} It consumes the same contracts and

services as other products; it is not an authority layer.\allowbreak{}


AIDE and Codex are repo/\allowbreak{}control-\allowbreak{}plane harnesses and bounded patch execution

surfaces.\allowbreak{} They help operate the repository; they do not replace canon,

contracts, validation, or evidence.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{What This Is Not}

Dominium is not a monolithic game executable, a renderer-\allowbreak{}owned simulation, a

traditional mode-\allowbreak{}flag game, a silent fallback system, or a place where generated

output becomes source truth by convenience.\allowbreak{}


It is also not currently release-\allowbreak{}ready.\allowbreak{} Full CTest and broader release/\allowbreak{}trust

proof remain visible debt outside the normal fast strict development gate.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{Core Invariants}

\begin{itemize}
\item Determinism first: identical canonical inputs produce identical authoritative
\end{itemize}
outputs.\allowbreak{}

\begin{itemize}
\item Process-\allowbreak{}only mutation: authoritative truth changes only through lawful,
\end{itemize}
deterministic Process execution.\allowbreak{}

\begin{itemize}
\item Truth /\allowbreak{} perceived /\allowbreak{} render separation: truth is authoritative; perception is
\end{itemize}
law-\allowbreak{}filtered; rendering is presentation only.\allowbreak{}

\begin{itemize}
\item Profiles over mode flags: behavior composition comes from profiles, bundles,
\end{itemize}
law surfaces, and constraints, not hardcoded runtime mode forks.\allowbreak{}

\begin{itemize}
\item Explicit refusal: unsupported or invalid transitions return deterministic,
\end{itemize}
auditable refusal.\allowbreak{}

\begin{itemize}
\item Pack-\allowbreak{}driven integration: optional content and capabilities are declared by
\end{itemize}
packs, contracts, registries, and compatibility law.\allowbreak{}

\begin{itemize}
\item Public identity is contractual: paths and implementations are not public
\end{itemize}
surfaces unless registered as such.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{Semantic Spine}

The reusable truth is not a button, screen, renderer, or tool.\allowbreak{} The reusable truth

is the contract-\allowbreak{}governed surface:


\vonecode{intent\par
-\allowbreak{}> command\par
-\allowbreak{}> capability/\allowbreak{}refusal check\par
-\allowbreak{}> service or deterministic process\par
-\allowbreak{}> result | document | snapshot\par
-\allowbreak{}> diagnostics/\allowbreak{}evidence\par
-\allowbreak{}> view/\allowbreak{}action model\par
-\allowbreak{}> projection\par
-\allowbreak{}> shell\par}

CLI, text/\allowbreak{}TUI, rendered GUI, native GUI, headless reports, Workbench panels, CI,

and AIDE should project the same command/\allowbreak{}result/\allowbreak{}refusal/\allowbreak{}diagnostic/\allowbreak{}evidence

truth rather than inventing separate product behavior.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{Product Shape}

\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{apps/\allowbreak{}client/\allowbreak{}}: client product composition, input, perception, and
\end{itemize}
presentation shell.\allowbreak{}

\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{apps/\allowbreak{}server/\allowbreak{}}: authoritative server product composition and admin/\allowbreak{}headless
\end{itemize}
surfaces.\allowbreak{}

\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{apps/\allowbreak{}launcher/\allowbreak{}}: profiles, instances, compatibility, and launch
\end{itemize}
orchestration.\allowbreak{}

\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{apps/\allowbreak{}setup/\allowbreak{}}: install, repair, rollback, and local product configuration.\allowbreak{}
\item \texttt{apps/\allowbreak{}workbench/\allowbreak{}}: governed validation, evidence, inspection, and later
\end{itemize}
authoring workflows.\allowbreak{}

\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{tools/\allowbreak{}}: validators, migration tools, packaging helpers, codegen, audit, and
\end{itemize}
developer machinery.\allowbreak{}


Apps compose.\allowbreak{} Runtime implements reusable behavior.\allowbreak{} Contracts define law.\allowbreak{}

Content supplies authored payload.\allowbreak{} Tools validate, generate, migrate, and audit.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{Repository Map}

\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{apps/\allowbreak{}}: thin product entrypoints and product composition.\allowbreak{}
\item \texttt{engine/\allowbreak{}}: Domino deterministic substrate and public engine-\allowbreak{}facing surfaces.\allowbreak{}
\item \texttt{game/\allowbreak{}}: Dominium domain rules, process emission, and game interpretation.\allowbreak{}
\item \texttt{runtime/\allowbreak{}}: AppShell, platform, shell, UI/\allowbreak{}projection adapters, diagnostics,
\end{itemize}
storage, input, audio, network, and host integration.\allowbreak{}

\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{contracts/\allowbreak{}}: machine-\allowbreak{}readable, version-\allowbreak{}pinned, compatibility-\allowbreak{}sensitive law.\allowbreak{}
\item \texttt{content/\allowbreak{}}: authored packs, profiles, datasets, fixtures-\allowbreak{}as-\allowbreak{}content, assets,
\end{itemize}
templates, and source content payloads.\allowbreak{}

\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}}: canon, architecture, development, reference, planning, release, and
\end{itemize}
repo documentation.\allowbreak{}

\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{tests/\allowbreak{}}: contract, invariant, smoke, integration, fixture, and proof suites.\allowbreak{}
\item \texttt{tools/\allowbreak{}}: repo-\allowbreak{}only validation, packaging, migration, release, audit, and
\end{itemize}
developer tooling.\allowbreak{}

\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{archive/\allowbreak{}}: historical, superseded, quarantined, or provenance-\allowbreak{}retained
\end{itemize}
material.\allowbreak{}


Ownership-\allowbreak{}sensitive split reminders:


\begin{itemize}
\item Do not infer ownership from similarly named roots.\allowbreak{}
\item Follow \texttt{AGENTS.\allowbreak{}md} and scope-\allowbreak{}specific contract/\allowbreak{}planning artifacts before
\end{itemize}
binding new work to transitional, projected, or quarantined roots.\allowbreak{}

\begin{itemize}
\item Generated outputs are evidence unless a stronger source promotes them.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{Language And Platform Baseline}

Mainline source uses:


\begin{itemize}
\item C17 for C code.\allowbreak{}
\item C++17 for C++ code.\allowbreak{}
\item C-\allowbreak{}compatible public ABI boundaries for stable binary-\allowbreak{}facing surfaces.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

The active portability floor includes Windows 7 SP1, macOS 10.\allowbreak{}9.\allowbreak{}5, and Linux.\allowbreak{}

C++17 language mode is allowed, but public ABI surfaces do not expose C++

classes, STL types, exceptions, RTTI, allocator objects, or compiler object

layout.\allowbreak{}


See:


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}development/\allowbreak{}LANGUAGE\_\allowbreak{}BASELINE.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}development/\allowbreak{}C17\_\allowbreak{}USAGE\_\allowbreak{}POLICY.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}development/\allowbreak{}CPP17\_\allowbreak{}USAGE\_\allowbreak{}POLICY.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}development/\allowbreak{}MACOS\_\allowbreak{}10\_\allowbreak{}9\_\allowbreak{}CPP17\_\allowbreak{}LIBRARY\_\allowbreak{}SUBSET.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{contracts/\allowbreak{}abi/\allowbreak{}c\_\allowbreak{}api.\allowbreak{}contract.\allowbreak{}toml}
\item \texttt{contracts/\allowbreak{}abi/\allowbreak{}language\_\allowbreak{}boundary.\allowbreak{}contract.\allowbreak{}toml}
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{Build And Verify}

Configure and build the normal verify preset:


\vonecode{cmake -\allowbreak{}-\allowbreak{}preset verify\par
cmake -\allowbreak{}-\allowbreak{}build -\allowbreak{}-\allowbreak{}preset verify -\allowbreak{}-\allowbreak{}target ALL\_\allowbreak{}BUILD\par}

Run the normal development proof gate:


\vonecode{py -\allowbreak{}3 tools/\allowbreak{}test/\allowbreak{}run\_\allowbreak{}fast\_\allowbreak{}strict.\allowbreak{}py -\allowbreak{}-\allowbreak{}repo-\allowbreak{}root .\allowbreak{}\par}

Run AIDE local health checks:


\vonecode{py -\allowbreak{}3 .\allowbreak{}aide/\allowbreak{}scripts/\allowbreak{}aide\_\allowbreak{}lite.\allowbreak{}py doctor\par
py -\allowbreak{}3 .\allowbreak{}aide/\allowbreak{}scripts/\allowbreak{}aide\_\allowbreak{}lite.\allowbreak{}py validate\par}

Run targeted contract validators as needed:


\vonecode{py -\allowbreak{}3 tools/\allowbreak{}validators/\allowbreak{}repo/\allowbreak{}check\_\allowbreak{}dependency\_\allowbreak{}directions.\allowbreak{}py -\allowbreak{}-\allowbreak{}repo-\allowbreak{}root .\allowbreak{} -\allowbreak{}-\allowbreak{}strict\par
py -\allowbreak{}3 tools/\allowbreak{}validators/\allowbreak{}contracts/\allowbreak{}check\_\allowbreak{}command\_\allowbreak{}surface.\allowbreak{}py -\allowbreak{}-\allowbreak{}repo-\allowbreak{}root .\allowbreak{} -\allowbreak{}-\allowbreak{}strict\par
py -\allowbreak{}3 tools/\allowbreak{}validators/\allowbreak{}contracts/\allowbreak{}check\_\allowbreak{}module\_\allowbreak{}descriptors.\allowbreak{}py -\allowbreak{}-\allowbreak{}repo-\allowbreak{}root .\allowbreak{} -\allowbreak{}-\allowbreak{}strict\par
py -\allowbreak{}3 tools/\allowbreak{}validators/\allowbreak{}contracts/\allowbreak{}check\_\allowbreak{}diagnostics\_\allowbreak{}registry.\allowbreak{}py -\allowbreak{}-\allowbreak{}repo-\allowbreak{}root .\allowbreak{} -\allowbreak{}-\allowbreak{}strict\par}

Fast strict is the normal development gate.\allowbreak{} Extended, release, and full proof

tiers are separate gates defined by \texttt{contracts/\allowbreak{}testing/\allowbreak{}test\_\allowbreak{}tiers.\allowbreak{}contract.\allowbreak{}toml}.\allowbreak{}

A green fast strict result does not claim full certification.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{Contracts And Public Surfaces}

Public identity must be registered and versioned.\allowbreak{} A file path, implementation,

or generated artifact is not public merely because it exists.\allowbreak{}


Core contract entrypoints:


\begin{itemize}
\item Public surfaces: \texttt{contracts/\allowbreak{}public\_\allowbreak{}surface/\allowbreak{}public\_\allowbreak{}surface.\allowbreak{}contract.\allowbreak{}toml}
\item Commands: \texttt{contracts/\allowbreak{}command/\allowbreak{}command\_\allowbreak{}surface.\allowbreak{}contract.\allowbreak{}toml}
\item Views: \texttt{contracts/\allowbreak{}view/\allowbreak{}view\_\allowbreak{}surface.\allowbreak{}contract.\allowbreak{}toml}
\item Diagnostics: \texttt{contracts/\allowbreak{}diagnostic/\allowbreak{}diagnostic\_\allowbreak{}code.\allowbreak{}registry.\allowbreak{}json}
\item Refusals: \texttt{contracts/\allowbreak{}refusal/\allowbreak{}refusal\_\allowbreak{}code.\allowbreak{}registry.\allowbreak{}json}
\item Capabilities: \texttt{contracts/\allowbreak{}capability/\allowbreak{}capability.\allowbreak{}registry.\allowbreak{}json}
\item Modules: \texttt{contracts/\allowbreak{}module/\allowbreak{}module\_\allowbreak{}surface.\allowbreak{}contract.\allowbreak{}toml}
\item Providers: \texttt{contracts/\allowbreak{}provider/\allowbreak{}provider.\allowbreak{}contract.\allowbreak{}toml}
\item Services: \texttt{contracts/\allowbreak{}service/\allowbreak{}service.\allowbreak{}contract.\allowbreak{}toml}
\item Project graph: \texttt{contracts/\allowbreak{}project\_\allowbreak{}graph/\allowbreak{}project\_\allowbreak{}graph\_\allowbreak{}model.\allowbreak{}contract.\allowbreak{}toml}
\item Packages and packs: \texttt{contracts/\allowbreak{}package/\allowbreak{}}
\item Replay proof: \texttt{contracts/\allowbreak{}replay/\allowbreak{}}
\end{itemize}

When behavior or compatibility meaning changes, update the relevant contract

surface and proof in the same task.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{Content, Packs, And Modding}

Content is authored data, not runtime law.\allowbreak{} Packs and registries describe optional

content, capabilities, compatibility, activation, and distribution surfaces.\allowbreak{}

Missing optional content must degrade or refuse explicitly.\allowbreak{}


Start with:


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{MODDING.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{content/\allowbreak{}README.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{content/\allowbreak{}packs/\allowbreak{}README.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{contracts/\allowbreak{}package/\allowbreak{}packs/\allowbreak{}README.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{contracts/\allowbreak{}capability/\allowbreak{}README.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}

Early pack tiers should remain data-\allowbreak{}first.\allowbreak{} Arbitrary executable code in packs is

not part of the current trust model.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{Documentation Map}

Use canon and contracts first, then architecture and development docs for

implementation guidance.\allowbreak{}


\begin{itemize}
\item Product overview: \texttt{DOMINIUM.\allowbreak{}md}
\item Documentation root: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}README.\allowbreak{}md}
\item Canonical system map: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}CANONICAL\_\allowbreak{}SYSTEM\_\allowbreak{}MAP.\allowbreak{}md}
\item Services and products: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}SERVICES\_\allowbreak{}AND\_\allowbreak{}PRODUCTS.\allowbreak{}md}
\item Foundation status: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}repo/\allowbreak{}FOUNDATION\_\allowbreak{}LOCK.\allowbreak{}md}
\item Current queue: \texttt{.\allowbreak{}aide/\allowbreak{}queue/\allowbreak{}current.\allowbreak{}toml}
\item Workbench validation slice: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}repo/\allowbreak{}audits/\allowbreak{}WORKBENCH\_\allowbreak{}VALIDATION\_\allowbreak{}SLICE\_\allowbreak{}01.\allowbreak{}md}
\item Document/\allowbreak{}patch transactions: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}document\_\allowbreak{}patch\_\allowbreak{}transaction.\allowbreak{}md}
\item Project graph service: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}project\_\allowbreak{}graph\_\allowbreak{}service.\allowbreak{}md}
\item Build matrix: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}development/\allowbreak{}BUILD\_\allowbreak{}MATRIX.\allowbreak{}md}
\item Build guide: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}development/\allowbreak{}guides/\allowbreak{}BUILDING.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}

Old docs are retained for provenance, but canon, glossary, AGENTS, active

contracts, current queue state, and reviewed audits outrank stale references.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{Contributing}

Before substantive work, identify the governing class and authority documents.\allowbreak{}

Use the task invocation shape from \texttt{AGENTS.\allowbreak{}md}:


\vonecode{Task:\par
Goal:\par
Touched Paths:\par
Relevant Invariants:\par
Contracts/\allowbreak{}Schemas:\par
Validation Level: FAST | STRICT | FULL\par
Expected Artifacts:\par
Non-\allowbreak{}Goals:\par}

For ordinary bounded work:


\begin{enumerate}
\item Read the relevant canon, contract, and ownership documents.\allowbreak{}
\item Keep edits in the owning root.\allowbreak{}
\item Update contracts/\allowbreak{}schemas when behavior or compatibility meaning changes.\allowbreak{}
\item Run targeted validation plus \texttt{git diff -\allowbreak{}-\allowbreak{}check}.\allowbreak{}
\item Run fast strict when scope warrants it or when claiming gate status.\allowbreak{}
\item Report what was run and what was not run.\allowbreak{}
\end{enumerate}

See \texttt{CONTRIBUTING.\allowbreak{}md} for contributor workflow notes, but resolve conflicts

against canon, glossary, AGENTS, and active contracts.\allowbreak{}

\item Security policy: \texttt{SECURITY.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}



\section{Dominium Documentation}

\vonecallout{DomSlate}{Source}{\texttt{current} \texttt{human\_\allowbreak{}full\_\allowbreak{}text} \texttt{unknown\_\allowbreak{}or\_\allowbreak{}unclassified} Source: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}README.\allowbreak{}md}.\allowbreak{} Reason: current high-\allowbreak{}authority orientation source.\allowbreak{}}

Future Series: DOC-\allowbreak{}CONVERGENCE

Replacement Target: patched document aligned to current canon ownership and release scope


\subsection{Dominium Documentation}

\subsubsection{Patch Notes}

\begin{itemize}
\item Current status: partially aligned to the Constitutional Architecture and release-\allowbreak{}freeze documentation set.\allowbreak{}
\item Required updates: documentation surface exists, but current canon ownership is not explicit
\item Cross-\allowbreak{}check with: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}archive/\allowbreak{}audit/\allowbreak{}CANON\_\allowbreak{}MAP.\allowbreak{}md} and \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}archive/\allowbreak{}audit/\allowbreak{}DOC\_\allowbreak{}DRIFT\_\allowbreak{}MATRIX.\allowbreak{}md}.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Status: current.\allowbreak{}

Scope: high-\allowbreak{}level orientation and map.\allowbreak{}


Normative contracts live under \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}} only.\allowbreak{} All other docs are

guidance, reference, or historical context.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{Core mental model}

\begin{itemize}
\item The simulation kernel is the source of truth; perception layers are derived.\allowbreak{}
\item Objective snapshots record authoritative state; subjective snapshots record views.\allowbreak{}
\item Packs provide capabilities, data, and assets; executables do not embed content.\allowbreak{}
\item Determinism and replay-\allowbreak{}first design are mandatory.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{Where to start}

\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}WHAT\_\allowbreak{}THIS\_\allowbreak{}IS.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}WHAT\_\allowbreak{}THIS\_\allowbreak{}IS\_\allowbreak{}NOT.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}INVARIANTS.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}CANONICAL\_\allowbreak{}SYSTEM\_\allowbreak{}MAP.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}CONTRACTS\_\allowbreak{}INDEX.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{Documentation taxonomy}

\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}} binding contracts and laws
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}release/\allowbreak{}roadmap/\allowbreak{}} goals and coverage tests only
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}content/\allowbreak{}} data and pack explanation only
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}development/\allowbreak{}} developer how-\allowbreak{}to only
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}modding/\allowbreak{}} modding how-\allowbreak{}to only
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}archive/\allowbreak{}} historical and superseded docs only
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{Archival notes}

Archived documents are kept for provenance only.\allowbreak{} Canonical contracts are in

\texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}}.\allowbreak{}




\section{Dominium Agent Governance}

\vonecallout{DomSlate}{Source}{\texttt{current} \texttt{human\_\allowbreak{}full\_\allowbreak{}text} \texttt{current\_\allowbreak{}repo\_\allowbreak{}truth} Source: \texttt{AGENTS.\allowbreak{}md}.\allowbreak{} Reason: required high-\allowbreak{}authority orientation source.\allowbreak{}}

Future Series: Sigma-\allowbreak{}1, Sigma-\allowbreak{}2, Sigma-\allowbreak{}3, Sigma-\allowbreak{}4, Sigma-\allowbreak{}5, Phi, Upsilon, Zeta

Replacement Target: none; later mirrors and machine-\allowbreak{}readable governance surfaces must derive from this file rather than compete with it

Binding Sources: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}canon/\allowbreak{}constitution\_\allowbreak{}v1.\allowbreak{}md}, \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}canon/\allowbreak{}glossary\_\allowbreak{}v1.\allowbreak{}md}, \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}planning/\allowbreak{}AUTHORITY\_\allowbreak{}ORDER.\allowbreak{}md}, \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}planning/\allowbreak{}POST\_\allowbreak{}PI\_\allowbreak{}EXECUTION\_\allowbreak{}PLAN.\allowbreak{}md}, \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}planning/\allowbreak{}EXTEND\_\allowbreak{}NOT\_\allowbreak{}REPLACE\_\allowbreak{}LEDGER.\allowbreak{}md}, \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}planning/\allowbreak{}GATES\_\allowbreak{}AND\_\allowbreak{}PROOFS.\allowbreak{}md}, \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}planning/\allowbreak{}SEMANTIC\_\allowbreak{}OWNERSHIP\_\allowbreak{}REVIEW.\allowbreak{}md}


\subsection{Dominium Agent Governance}

\subsubsection{1. Purpose And Scope}

\texttt{AGENTS.\allowbreak{}md} is the single canonical governance source for how humans, GPT/\allowbreak{}Codex agents, Claude-\allowbreak{}style agents, Copilot-\allowbreak{}style agents, MCP-\allowbreak{}mediated tools, and future execution prompts are allowed to operate in this repository.\allowbreak{}


It governs:


\begin{itemize}
\item authority precedence for repo-\allowbreak{}grounded work
\item current program-\allowbreak{}state orientation for post-\allowbreak{}\texttt{Lambda} execution
\item core operating rules and non-\allowbreak{}negotiable execution constraints
\item high-\allowbreak{}level work classes
\item validation and reporting expectations
\item review-\allowbreak{}gated and ownership-\allowbreak{}sensitive areas
\end{itemize}

It does not yet define:


\begin{itemize}
\item generated mirrors or vendor-\allowbreak{}specific instruction surfaces
\item the natural-\allowbreak{}language task bridge
\item the XStack task catalog
\item MCP exposure contracts
\item the final hardened agent safety policy
\end{itemize}

Those later surfaces must inherit from this file instead of inventing a parallel governance canon.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{2. Authority Model}

When repo artifacts, mirrors, generated outputs, and chat memory differ, use the following rule:


\begin{enumerate}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}canon/\allowbreak{}constitution\_\allowbreak{}v1.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}canon/\allowbreak{}glossary\_\allowbreak{}v1.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{AGENTS.\allowbreak{}md}
\item scope-\allowbreak{}specific canonical planning, semantic, schema, contract, release, and policy artifacts named by the active task
\item operational registries, projections, mirrors, manifests, and generated evidence with intact provenance
\item chat summaries, remembered transcript claims, and uncommitted planning notes
\end{enumerate}

The governing consequences are:


\begin{itemize}
\item repo artifacts outrank chat memory
\item canon and glossary outrank all lower-\allowbreak{}level prose
\item mirrors are derived, not canonical
\item generated outputs are evidence only unless a stronger source explicitly promotes them
\item if repo artifacts conflict materially, resolve the conflict with \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}planning/\allowbreak{}AUTHORITY\_\allowbreak{}ORDER.\allowbreak{}md} and \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}planning/\allowbreak{}SNAPSHOT\_\allowbreak{}INTAKE\_\allowbreak{}PROTOCOL.\allowbreak{}md} rather than by convenience
\item chat summaries may orient work, but they may not override repo truth
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{3. Current Program State}

The current committed execution position is:


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{Omega}, \texttt{Xi}, and \texttt{Pi} complete
\item \texttt{P-\allowbreak{}0} through \texttt{P-\allowbreak{}4} complete
\item \texttt{0-\allowbreak{}0} planning hardening complete
\item \texttt{Lambda-\allowbreak{}0} through \texttt{Lambda-\allowbreak{}6} complete
\item current checkpoint: \texttt{post-\allowbreak{}Lambda /\allowbreak{} pre-\allowbreak{}Sigma-\allowbreak{}A}
\item current executable prompt: \texttt{Sigma-\allowbreak{}0}
\item current execution block: \texttt{Sigma-\allowbreak{}A}
\end{itemize}

Governance work must therefore consume the completed \texttt{Lambda} doctrine rather than invent a new semantic baseline.\allowbreak{}


Continuity note:


\begin{itemize}
\item some older planning artifacts still retain pre-\allowbreak{}\texttt{Sigma} or earlier \texttt{Sigma} ordering text
\item for governance execution, treat the active executable prompt and this file as the canonical post-\allowbreak{}\texttt{Lambda} governance baseline until downstream planning mirrors are refreshed
\item do not silently rewrite broader planning artifacts just to erase that drift unless a prompt explicitly targets them
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{4. Core Operating Rules}

All humans and agents operating in this repo must follow these rules:


\begin{itemize}
\item extend over replace unless stronger doctrine or explicit human direction says otherwise
\item do not introduce silent semantic drift
\item do not bypass authority ordering, gate logic, or review checkpoints
\item do not infer canon from convenience, shared code, or generated output shape
\item do not replace repo truth with chat summaries or remembered intent
\item do not silently rebind work to projected, generated, transitional, or quarantined roots
\item planning-\allowbreak{}only prompts do not authorize runtime, refactor, or implementation work
\item implementation-\allowbreak{}facing prompts do not authorize doctrine rewrites unless they explicitly target doctrine
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{5. Constitutional Execution Floor}

The following inherited rules remain non-\allowbreak{}negotiable:


\paragraph{5.1 No mode flags; profiles only}

\begin{itemize}
\item do not add or preserve hardcoded runtime mode branches
\item express behavior composition through profiles, bundles, law surfaces, and explicit constraints
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{5.2 Process-only mutation}

\begin{itemize}
\item authoritative truth mutation must occur through lawful deterministic Process execution
\item UI, render, operator, tooling, or convenience layers must not mutate truth directly
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{5.3 Truth / Perceived / Render separation}

\begin{itemize}
\item truth is authoritative
\item perception and observation are filtered views
\item rendering is presentation only
\item later governance and tool work must not collapse those layers
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{5.4 Pack-driven integration}

\begin{itemize}
\item optional content and capabilities must remain pack-\allowbreak{} and registry-\allowbreak{}driven
\item missing packs require explicit refusal or degradation rather than hidden fallback magic
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{5.5 Determinism discipline}

\begin{itemize}
\item use named RNG streams for authoritative randomness
\item preserve thread-\allowbreak{}count invariance, deterministic ordering, and deterministic reductions
\item preserve replay-\allowbreak{}hash equivalence for canonical partitions where applicable
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{5.6 Contract and compatibility discipline}

\begin{itemize}
\item respect explicit schema identity, version, stability, migration, and refusal obligations
\item do not perform silent migrations or compatibility reinterpretation
\item update contract-\allowbreak{}facing docs when behavior or compatibility meaning changes
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{6. Required Doctrine Inputs Before Acting}

Before substantive work, agents must consult the relevant authoritative repo artifacts for the task.\allowbreak{} At minimum, the normal doctrine packet is:


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}canon/\allowbreak{}constitution\_\allowbreak{}v1.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}canon/\allowbreak{}glossary\_\allowbreak{}v1.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{AGENTS.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}planning/\allowbreak{}SNAPSHOT\_\allowbreak{}INTAKE\_\allowbreak{}PROTOCOL.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}planning/\allowbreak{}AUTHORITY\_\allowbreak{}ORDER.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}planning/\allowbreak{}MERGED\_\allowbreak{}PROGRAM\_\allowbreak{}STATE.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}planning/\allowbreak{}EXTEND\_\allowbreak{}NOT\_\allowbreak{}REPLACE\_\allowbreak{}LEDGER.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}planning/\allowbreak{}GATES\_\allowbreak{}AND\_\allowbreak{}PROOFS.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}planning/\allowbreak{}POST\_\allowbreak{}PI\_\allowbreak{}EXECUTION\_\allowbreak{}PLAN.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}planning/\allowbreak{}SEMANTIC\_\allowbreak{}OWNERSHIP\_\allowbreak{}REVIEW.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}planning/\allowbreak{}PLAYER\_\allowbreak{}DESIRE\_\allowbreak{}ACCEPTANCE\_\allowbreak{}MAP.\allowbreak{}md}
\item the relevant \texttt{Lambda} semantic constitution artifacts under \texttt{specs/\allowbreak{}reality/\allowbreak{}} and \texttt{data/\allowbreak{}reality/\allowbreak{}}
\item \texttt{contracts/\allowbreak{}planning/\allowbreak{}final\_\allowbreak{}prompt\_\allowbreak{}inventory.\allowbreak{}json}
\item \texttt{contracts/\allowbreak{}planning/\allowbreak{}dependency\_\allowbreak{}graph\_\allowbreak{}post\_\allowbreak{}pi.\allowbreak{}json}
\end{itemize}

Task-\allowbreak{}specific additions are mandatory when scope expands:


\begin{itemize}
\item schema or compatibility work: \texttt{schema/\allowbreak{}**}, \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}reference/\allowbreak{}contracts/\allowbreak{}**}, compat metadata
\item release or control-\allowbreak{}plane work: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}release/\allowbreak{}**}, \texttt{contracts/\allowbreak{}repo/\allowbreak{}release\_\allowbreak{}policy.\allowbreak{}toml}, release and update registries
\item runtime extraction work: relevant runtime roots plus ownership review and bridge law
\item bridge or ownership-\allowbreak{}sensitive work: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}planning/\allowbreak{}SEMANTIC\_\allowbreak{}OWNERSHIP\_\allowbreak{}REVIEW.\allowbreak{}md} before binding to overlapping roots
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{7. Work Classes}

The repository recognizes these high-\allowbreak{}level work classes:


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{planning}: sequencing, checkpoints, inventories, dependency maps, gates, and continuity work
\item \texttt{doctrine\_\allowbreak{}spec}: normative constitutional, contract, or specification work
\item \texttt{governance}: agent, operator, instruction, refusal, and review-\allowbreak{}surface work
\item \texttt{semantic\_\allowbreak{}domain}: reality, domain, capability, representation, formalization, or bridge work
\item \texttt{runtime\_\allowbreak{}platform}: kernel, component, event, service, persistence, sandbox, or platform-\allowbreak{}boundary work
\item \texttt{release\_\allowbreak{}control\_\allowbreak{}plane}: release, build, versioning, identity, trust, archive, publication, or control-\allowbreak{}plane work
\item \texttt{packaging\_\allowbreak{}checkpointing}: bundle, report, manifest, and checkpoint-\allowbreak{}curation work
\item \texttt{validation\_\allowbreak{}audit}: verification, consistency, evidence, audit, and proof work
\item \texttt{refactor\_\allowbreak{}convergence}: physical convergence, replacement, merge-\allowbreak{}later, or structure-\allowbreak{}normalization work
\end{itemize}

High-\allowbreak{}level task intent mapping is refined later.\allowbreak{} This file only defines the canonical class vocabulary and the minimum expectations attached to each class.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{8. Validation And Reporting Expectations}

Before claiming success, agents must:


\begin{enumerate}
\item state the relevant invariant documents or IDs being upheld
\item state whether contract or schema impact changed
\item use \texttt{FAST} validation at minimum unless the task is docs-\allowbreak{}only and explicitly exempt from stronger checks
\item verify that the target artifacts required by the prompt exist
\item parse touched JSON or schema artifacts where relevant
\item check internal consistency between prose and machine-\allowbreak{}readable mirrors when both are produced
\item run \texttt{git diff -\allowbreak{}-\allowbreak{}check}
\item report what was run and what was not run
\item avoid claiming implementation progress on planning-\allowbreak{}only prompts
\end{enumerate}

Validation strength must increase when task scope increases.\allowbreak{} A docs-\allowbreak{}only task does not excuse false claims about unrun runtime or build checks.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{9. Review-Gated And Protected Areas}

Explicit human review is required for work that:


\begin{itemize}
\item changes canon doctrine or glossary meaning
\item reinterprets authority ordering, intake law, or this governance baseline
\item touches replace-\allowbreak{}classified or do-\allowbreak{}not-\allowbreak{}replace surfaces in ways that exceed the prompt
\item crosses unresolved or quarantined ownership areas
\item changes release, publication, licensing, trust, or public policy meaning
\item enters live-\allowbreak{}ops or \texttt{Zeta}-\allowbreak{}class territory
\item alters foundational semantic meaning without an explicit doctrine-\allowbreak{}update prompt
\end{itemize}

Protected or caution-\allowbreak{}heavy zones include:


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}canon/\allowbreak{}**}
\item \texttt{AGENTS.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}planning/\allowbreak{}AUTHORITY\_\allowbreak{}ORDER.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}planning/\allowbreak{}SNAPSHOT\_\allowbreak{}INTAKE\_\allowbreak{}PROTOCOL.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}planning/\allowbreak{}MERGED\_\allowbreak{}PROGRAM\_\allowbreak{}STATE.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}planning/\allowbreak{}EXTEND\_\allowbreak{}NOT\_\allowbreak{}REPLACE\_\allowbreak{}LEDGER.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}planning/\allowbreak{}GATES\_\allowbreak{}AND\_\allowbreak{}PROOFS.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{specs/\allowbreak{}reality/\allowbreak{}**}
\item \texttt{schema/\allowbreak{}**}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}release/\allowbreak{}**}
\item \texttt{release/\allowbreak{}**}, \texttt{repo/\allowbreak{}**}, \texttt{updates/\allowbreak{}**}, \texttt{security/\allowbreak{}**}
\item generated echoes under \texttt{build/\allowbreak{}**}, \texttt{archive/\allowbreak{}generated/\allowbreak{}artifacts/\allowbreak{}**}, \texttt{.\allowbreak{}xstack\_\allowbreak{}cache/\allowbreak{}**}, and \texttt{run\_\allowbreak{}meta/\allowbreak{}**}
\end{itemize}

Protected does not mean untouchable.\allowbreak{} It means explicit scope, review awareness, and provenance discipline are required.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{10. Ownership And Projection Cautions}

Agents must not assume the following ownership-\allowbreak{}sensitive roots are equivalent peers:


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{fields/\allowbreak{}} is canonical semantic field substrate; \texttt{field/\allowbreak{}} is a transitional compatibility facade
\item \texttt{schema/\allowbreak{}} is canonical semantic contract law; \texttt{schemas/\allowbreak{}} is a validator-\allowbreak{}facing projection or advisory mirror
\item \texttt{packs/\allowbreak{}} is canonical in runtime packaging, activation, compatibility, and distribution-\allowbreak{}descriptor scope
\item \texttt{data/\allowbreak{}packs/\allowbreak{}} remains authoritative within authored pack content and declaration scope, but stays transitional and residual-\allowbreak{}quarantined for any attempted single-\allowbreak{}root convergence
\item \texttt{specs/\allowbreak{}reality/\allowbreak{}} is canonical over \texttt{data/\allowbreak{}reality/\allowbreak{}}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}planning/\allowbreak{}} is canonical over \texttt{data/\allowbreak{}planning/\allowbreak{}}
\end{itemize}

Agents may not:


\begin{itemize}
\item silently bind new governance, runtime, task, or bridge work to the wrong side of those splits
\item treat projections as semantic owners because they are easier to consume
\item collapse residual quarantine into certainty by naming preference
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{11. Relation To Later Sigma Work}

This file is intentionally canonical but not overloaded.\allowbreak{}


Later \texttt{Sigma} prompts refine derived surfaces only:


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{Sigma-\allowbreak{}1} generates governance mirrors from this canonical source
\item \texttt{Sigma-\allowbreak{}2} formalizes high-\allowbreak{}level task intent and natural-\allowbreak{}language mapping
\item \texttt{Sigma-\allowbreak{}3} freezes the XStack task catalog
\item \texttt{Sigma-\allowbreak{}4} formalizes MCP and related interface exposure
\item \texttt{Sigma-\allowbreak{}5} hardens the agent safety policy
\end{itemize}

No later \texttt{Sigma} prompt may create a competing governance canon.\allowbreak{} They must refine or project this layer.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{12. Commit Discipline}

When tracked repository files change:


\begin{itemize}
\item make frequent commits at meaningful boundaries
\item use explicit, verbose, audit-\allowbreak{}grade commit messages
\item write commit messages that are sufficient to reconstruct a later changelog
\item do not invent commits for ignored or untracked checkpoint outputs only
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{13. Forbidden Moves}

The following moves are forbidden unless a prompt explicitly authorizes them and the required review conditions are met:


\begin{itemize}
\item creating a parallel canonical governance file
\item treating mirrors as canonical
\item bypassing doctrine to "just get it done"
\item replacing repo truth with prompt convenience or chat memory
\item refactoring code during planning-\allowbreak{}only work
\item binding runtime, governance, or release work to quarantined roots without review
\item silently promoting generated outputs into semantic authority
\item silently normalizing ownership drift because two roots look similar
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{AIDE Lite Portable Guidance}

\begin{itemize}
\item Use \texttt{.\allowbreak{}aide/\allowbreak{}context/\allowbreak{}latest-\allowbreak{}task-\allowbreak{}packet.\allowbreak{}md} as the default compact AIDE task brief when a task explicitly opts into AIDE Lite context.\allowbreak{}
\item Keep target-\allowbreak{}specific project state in \texttt{.\allowbreak{}aide/\allowbreak{}memory/\allowbreak{}}; do not copy source AIDE memory, queue history, generated context, reports, route decisions, cache-\allowbreak{}key reports, Gateway/\allowbreak{}provider status reports, \texttt{.\allowbreak{}aide.\allowbreak{}local/\allowbreak{}}, raw prompts, raw responses, or secrets.\allowbreak{}
\item Generate target-\allowbreak{}local context with \texttt{py -\allowbreak{}3 .\allowbreak{}aide/\allowbreak{}scripts/\allowbreak{}aide\_\allowbreak{}lite.\allowbreak{}py snapshot}, \texttt{index}, \texttt{context}, and \texttt{pack}; keep Dominium doctrine referenced by path instead of pasted into prompt memory.\allowbreak{}
\item Provider/\allowbreak{}model/\allowbreak{}network calls and Gateway forwarding remain forbidden unless a future reviewed Dominium task explicitly enables them.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}
<!-\allowbreak{}-\allowbreak{} AIDE-\allowbreak{}PORTABLE:END section=aide-\allowbreak{}lite-\allowbreak{}pack-\allowbreak{}v0 -\allowbreak{}-\allowbreak{}>

\end{itemize}
task packet points there.\allowbreak{}

\begin{itemize}
\item Do not paste long chat history, full repo dumps, raw prompts, raw responses,
\end{itemize}
secrets, provider keys, or \texttt{.\allowbreak{}aide.\allowbreak{}local/\allowbreak{}} contents.\allowbreak{}

\begin{itemize}

\end{itemize}
\texttt{validate}, and \texttt{pack -\allowbreak{}-\allowbreak{}task "<bounded task>"} when available.\allowbreak{}

\begin{itemize}
\item For quality-\allowbreak{}sensitive work, run \texttt{verify}, \texttt{review-\allowbreak{}pack}, \texttt{eval run}, and
\end{itemize}
evidence checks before review or promotion.\allowbreak{}

\begin{itemize}
\item For Q27-\allowbreak{}and-\allowbreak{}later work, use structured commits and run \texttt{commit check} when
\end{itemize}
practical.\allowbreak{}

\begin{itemize}
\item Inspect \texttt{task status} or \texttt{task inspect} before repeated, partial, or
\end{itemize}
out-\allowbreak{}of-\allowbreak{}order queue work.\allowbreak{}

\begin{itemize}
\item Run \texttt{git plan} before branch-\allowbreak{}sensitive work; do not mutate branches without
\end{itemize}
an explicit helper plan, validation evidence, and operator approval.\allowbreak{}

\begin{itemize}
\item Treat routine git/\allowbreak{}worktree drift as a mechanical blocker, not a terminal
\end{itemize}
stop: fetch or fast-\allowbreak{}forward when safe, preserve unrelated changes, continue

path-\allowbreak{}disjoint work, and create or resume an AIDE blocker-\allowbreak{}resolution task for

remaining drift.\allowbreak{}

\begin{itemize}
\item For validation, dependency, stale-\allowbreak{}generated-\allowbreak{}output, and dirty-\allowbreak{}tree blockers,
\end{itemize}
create or resume a bounded AIDE task before reporting blocked; ask the user

only for semantic authority conflicts, destructive ambiguity, missing

external secrets, or required review gates.\allowbreak{}

\begin{itemize}
\item Treat Gateway and provider surfaces as no-\allowbreak{}call/\allowbreak{}report-\allowbreak{}only unless a future
\end{itemize}
reviewed queue phase explicitly enables live execution.\allowbreak{}

\begin{itemize}
\item Write evidence, preserve manual content, stop at review gates, and report
\end{itemize}
validation honestly.\allowbreak{}

\section{Dominium Constitutional Architecture \& Execution Contract V1}

\vonecallout{DomSlate}{Source}{\texttt{current} \texttt{human\_\allowbreak{}full\_\allowbreak{}text} \texttt{canonical} Source: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}canon/\allowbreak{}constitution\_\allowbreak{}v1.\allowbreak{}md}.\allowbreak{} Reason: current high-\allowbreak{}authority orientation source.\allowbreak{}}

Future Series: DOC-\allowbreak{}ARCHIVE

Replacement Target: legacy reference surface retained without current binding authority


\subsection{Dominium Constitutional Architecture \& Execution Contract v1}

\subsubsection{1) Purpose}
This document is the binding constitutional contract for Dominium architecture and execution.\allowbreak{}

If any code, schema, tool, prompt, or documentation conflicts with this contract, this contract wins.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{2) Authority Order}
Apply this order when interpreting requirements:


\begin{enumerate}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}canon/\allowbreak{}constitution\_\allowbreak{}v1.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}canon/\allowbreak{}glossary\_\allowbreak{}v1.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{AGENTS.\allowbreak{}md} (repo root)
\item Schema law under \texttt{schema/\allowbreak{}} and contract docs under \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}reference/\allowbreak{}contracts/\allowbreak{}}
\item Architecture docs under \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}}
\item Roadmap and testing docs
\end{enumerate}

\subsubsection{3) Constitutional Axioms (Non-Negotiable)}

\paragraph{A1. Determinism is primary}
\begin{itemize}
\item Authoritative simulation outcomes MUST be identical for identical inputs.\allowbreak{}
\item Step-\allowbreak{}by-\allowbreak{}step and batched execution MUST remain equivalent.\allowbreak{}
\item Thread count, scheduler interleavings, and backend choice MUST NOT change authoritative outputs.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{A2. Process-only mutation}
\begin{itemize}
\item Authoritative state mutation MUST occur only through deterministic Process execution.\allowbreak{}
\item Direct writes outside Process commit boundaries are forbidden.\allowbreak{}
\item Tooling MAY request mutation only through lawful intent/\allowbreak{}process paths.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{A3. Law-gated authority}
\begin{itemize}
\item Capability grants permission to attempt; law determines accept/\allowbreak{}refuse/\allowbreak{}transform.\allowbreak{}
\item Authority does not bypass law.\allowbreak{}
\item Refusals are lawful outcomes and MUST be explicit, deterministic, and auditable.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{A4. No runtime mode flags}
\begin{itemize}
\item Runtime behavior MUST resolve from profile data (\texttt{ExperienceProfile}, \texttt{LawProfile}, \texttt{ParameterBundle}, optional \texttt{MissionSpec} constraints).\allowbreak{}
\item Hardcoded mode booleans/\allowbreak{}branches (for example \texttt{*\_\allowbreak{}mode} runtime forks) are forbidden.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{A5. Event-driven advancement}
\begin{itemize}
\item Simulation advances via scheduled events and deterministic task execution.\allowbreak{}
\item Hidden background mutation and global per-\allowbreak{}tick scans that mutate state are forbidden.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{A6. Provenance is mandatory}
\begin{itemize}
\item Creation, mutation, transfer, and destruction MUST have deterministic causal chains.\allowbreak{}
\item Save/\allowbreak{}replay/\allowbreak{}audit artifacts MUST preserve that provenance.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{A7. Observer-Renderer-Truth separation}
\begin{itemize}
\item Truth is authoritative state.\allowbreak{}
\item Perception is a law/\allowbreak{}authority/\allowbreak{}lens-\allowbreak{}filtered projection.\allowbreak{}
\item Rendering is presentational only and MUST NOT mutate truth or enforce authority decisions.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{A8. Engine/Game/Client/Server boundaries}
\begin{itemize}
\item Engine defines deterministic mechanisms.\allowbreak{}
\item Game defines rule meaning through engine contracts.\allowbreak{}
\item Client and renderer project data and issue intents; they do not author authoritative outcomes.\allowbreak{}
\item Server is authoritative in multiplayer and validates law/\allowbreak{}authority context.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{A9. Pack-driven integration}
\begin{itemize}
\item New content and capability surfaces integrate through packs and registries.\allowbreak{}
\item Packs are data-\allowbreak{}only and namespaced; executable code inside packs is forbidden.\allowbreak{}
\item Missing optional packs MUST produce deterministic refusal or deterministic degradation.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{A10. Explicit degradation and refusal}
\begin{itemize}
\item Budget pressure MAY defer/\allowbreak{}degrade/\allowbreak{}refuse.\allowbreak{}
\item Silent fallback is forbidden.\allowbreak{}
\item Degradation and refusal outcomes MUST be inspectable and auditable.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{A11. Absence is valid}
\begin{itemize}
\item Systems MUST remain lawful with optional subsystems absent (for example: no AI, no economy, no war).\allowbreak{}
\item Absence MUST produce explicit behavior, never hidden bypasses.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{4) Execution Contract (EXEC0 Family)}

\paragraph{E1. Work IR and Access IR}
\begin{itemize}
\item Authoritative work MUST be expressed as Work IR + Access IR contracts.\allowbreak{}
\item Task ordering keys, read/\allowbreak{}write/\allowbreak{}reduce declarations, and commit points MUST be explicit.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{E2. Deterministic ordering}
\begin{itemize}
\item Canonical commit key: \texttt{(phase\_\allowbreak{}id, task\_\allowbreak{}id, sub\_\allowbreak{}index)}.\allowbreak{}
\item Ordering decisions MUST be independent of hash-\allowbreak{}map iteration, pointer order, or thread completion order.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{E3. Deterministic reductions}
\begin{itemize}
\item Reductions MUST use fixed-\allowbreak{}tree deterministic reduction.\allowbreak{}
\item Float-\allowbreak{}based authoritative reductions are forbidden.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{E4. Named RNG streams}
\begin{itemize}
\item Authoritative randomness MUST use named streams.\allowbreak{}
\item Anonymous/\allowbreak{}global RNG and time-\allowbreak{}seeded randomness are forbidden.\allowbreak{}
\item Stream naming and derivation MUST follow deterministic RNG law.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{E5. Thread-count invariance}
\begin{itemize}
\item Authoritative outputs and partition hashes MUST remain invariant across allowed thread counts.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{E6. Replay equivalence}
\begin{itemize}
\item Replay from authoritative logs MUST reproduce canonical authoritative hashes.\allowbreak{}
\item Replay drift is a contract failure.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{E7. Hash-partition equivalence}
\begin{itemize}
\item Canonical partitions (\texttt{HASH\_\allowbreak{}SIM\_\allowbreak{}CORE}, \texttt{HASH\_\allowbreak{}SIM\_\allowbreak{}ECON}, \texttt{HASH\_\allowbreak{}SIM\_\allowbreak{}INFO}, \texttt{HASH\_\allowbreak{}SIM\_\allowbreak{}TIME}, \texttt{HASH\_\allowbreak{}SIM\_\allowbreak{}WORLD}) MUST match across equivalent runs.\allowbreak{}
\item Presentation hash divergence is non-\allowbreak{}authoritative unless explicitly promoted.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{E8. SRZ contract}
\begin{itemize}
\item Execution placement (server/\allowbreak{}delegated/\allowbreak{}dormant) changes where work runs, never what law permits.\allowbreak{}
\item Delegated execution requires deterministic proof artifacts before commit.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{E9. Commit legality}
\begin{itemize}
\item Any state transition that cannot be expressed under deterministic ordering, legal authority context, and auditable commit semantics is invalid.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{5) Compatibility, Schema, and Migration Obligations}

\paragraph{C1. Version semantics}
\begin{itemize}
\item All runtime-\allowbreak{}impacting schemas MUST declare \texttt{schema\_\allowbreak{}id}, \texttt{schema\_\allowbreak{}version}, and \texttt{stability}.\allowbreak{}
\item MAJOR changes require explicit migration routes or explicit refusal.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{C2. Skip-unknown preservation}
\begin{itemize}
\item Unknown fields MUST round-\allowbreak{}trip unchanged where contract says open-\allowbreak{}map/\allowbreak{}extension behavior.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{C3. CompatX obligations}
\begin{itemize}
\item Compatibility classes and migration links MUST be explicit and data-\allowbreak{}declared.\allowbreak{}
\item Breaking transitions require deterministic migration specs and tests.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\paragraph{C4. No silent coercion}
\begin{itemize}
\item Migration is explicit invoke-\allowbreak{}only.\allowbreak{}
\item Best-\allowbreak{}effort guessing, silent dropping, and implicit semantic defaulting are forbidden.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{6) Testing and Invariant Obligations Per Task}
Every non-\allowbreak{}trivial task MUST include:


\begin{enumerate}
\item Referenced invariants (by doc and section).\allowbreak{}
\item Contract impact statement (which schemas/\allowbreak{}contracts changed or confirmed unchanged).\allowbreak{}
\item Determinism impact statement (ordering, RNG, replay/\allowbreak{}hash partitions).\allowbreak{}
\item Validation execution (\texttt{FAST} at minimum, stricter when scope requires).\allowbreak{}
\item Document updates for any changed contractual behavior.\allowbreak{}
\end{enumerate}

\subsubsection{7) Refusal and Enforcement}
\begin{itemize}
\item Violations of constitutional invariants require refusal or rollback of the change request.\allowbreak{}
\item Workarounds that bypass invariants are forbidden.\allowbreak{}
\item Constitutional conflicts are resolved by this document, not by prompt convenience.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{8) Future Task Invocation Template}
Use this prompt block for future work so tasks remain short and stable:


\vonecode{Task ID:\par
Objective:\par
Touched Paths:\par
Relevant Invariants:\par
Required Contracts:\par
Required Validation Level: FAST | STRICT | FULL\par
Expected Artifacts:\par
Non-\allowbreak{}Goals:\par}

\subsubsection{9) Primary Cross-References}
\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}canon/\allowbreak{}glossary\_\allowbreak{}v1.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}ARCH0\_\allowbreak{}CONSTITUTION.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}PROCESS\_\allowbreak{}ONLY\_\allowbreak{}MUTATION.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}EXECUTION\_\allowbreak{}MODEL.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}EXECUTION\_\allowbreak{}REORDERING\_\allowbreak{}POLICY.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}DETERMINISTIC\_\allowbreak{}REDUCTION\_\allowbreak{}RULES.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}DETERMINISTIC\_\allowbreak{}ORDERING\_\allowbreak{}POLICY.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}RNG\_\allowbreak{}MODEL.\allowbreak{}md}

\section{Dominium Canonical Glossary V1.0.0}

\vonecallout{DomSlate}{Source}{\texttt{current} \texttt{human\_\allowbreak{}full\_\allowbreak{}text} \texttt{canonical} Source: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}canon/\allowbreak{}glossary\_\allowbreak{}v1.\allowbreak{}md}.\allowbreak{} Reason: current high-\allowbreak{}authority orientation source.\allowbreak{}}

Scope: Dominium /\allowbreak{} Domino ecosystem vocabulary.\allowbreak{}

Stability: stable

Future Series: DOC-\allowbreak{}ARCHIVE

Replacement Target: legacy reference surface retained without current binding authority


\subsection{Dominium Canonical Glossary v1.0.0}

This is the full canonical glossary v1.\allowbreak{}0.\allowbreak{}0.\allowbreak{}

If terminology conflicts with local or legacy docs, this glossary wins.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{Glossary Invariants}
\begin{itemize}
\item Terms in this document are canonical and binding for contracts, schemas, code comments, and prompts.\allowbreak{}
\item Deprecated terms must not be introduced in new runtime logic.\allowbreak{}
\item If a term is undefined here, it must not be treated as canonical until added through controlled update.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{Example Usage}
\vonecode{Correct: "The Observation Kernel maps TruthModel through Lens and AuthorityContext.\allowbreak{}"\par
Incorrect: "Renderer owns truth and can mutate state.\allowbreak{}"\par}

\subsubsection{TODO}
\begin{itemize}
\item Add a machine-\allowbreak{}readable term registry export format.\allowbreak{}
\item Add change-\allowbreak{}control procedure for glossary term additions/\allowbreak{}deprecations.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{Cross-References}
\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}canon/\allowbreak{}constitution\_\allowbreak{}v1.\allowbreak{}md}
\item \texttt{AGENTS.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{A}

\paragraph{Account}
A user identity external to the simulation ontology used for authentication, entitlements, and multiplayer coordination.\allowbreak{} An Account is not an Agent unless explicitly instantiated as one within the simulation.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Activation Policy}
A deterministic rule set defining when a Domain, Solver, or Micro-\allowbreak{}simulation may activate within a region of interest.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Agent}
An Assembly capable of submitting Intents under AuthorityContext and LawProfile constraints.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Architecture}
The structural layering of Dominium systems including Engine, Game, Client, Server, and XStack governance components.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Artifact}
A produced output from a build, verification, simulation, or governance process.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Artifact Class}
The classification of artifacts into Canonical, Derived, or Run-\allowbreak{}meta categories.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Authority}
Permission to execute Processes under Law.\allowbreak{} Authority is not power; it is validated capability within constraints.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{AuthorityContext}
The structured permission context required for all Process execution.\allowbreak{} Includes authority\_\allowbreak{}origin, law\_\allowbreak{}profile\_\allowbreak{}id, entitlements, epistemic\_\allowbreak{}scope, and privilege\_\allowbreak{}level.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{AuthorityOrigin}
The origin of authority: client, server, tool, replay, etc.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Authority tick}
The evaluation step where AuthorityContext is validated before Process execution.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{AuditX}
The static analysis subsystem within XStack responsible for detecting drift, anti-\allowbreak{}patterns, and semantic violations.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{B}

\paragraph{Bad}
Normatively incorrect or violating the Constitutional Architecture, invariants, or determinism.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Binary}
A compiled executable or library artifact.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Budget Envelope}
The deterministic compute constraints governing simulation cost per region, session, or tick.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Budget Policy}
A registry-\allowbreak{}driven configuration defining solver activation and fidelity under compute constraints.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Bug}
A deviation from deterministic, lawful, or architectural correctness.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Build}
The deterministic compilation and linking process producing Binaries.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Bundle}
A collection of Packs grouped for installation or activation.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{BundleProfile}
A declarative definition of grouped Packs, tools, or experiences.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{C}

\paragraph{Cache store}
Persistent content-\allowbreak{}addressed storage of verification or computation results keyed by input hash.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Canon}
The locked architectural truth of Dominium.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Canonical}
Conforming strictly to Canon and deterministic identity.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Canonical artifact}
A source-\allowbreak{}of-\allowbreak{}truth artifact that must not change without explicit migration.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Canonical hash}
A deterministic hash representing canonical state.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Capability}
A specific permission or affordance enabling a Process.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{CLI}
Command Line Interface.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Classroom-restricted}
A SecureX trust category restricting certain Packs or features to educational environments.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Client}
The application responsible for rendering, input capture, and presentation of PerceivedModel.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Collapse}
Reduction of simulation detail into a Macro Capsule while preserving invariants.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{CompatX}
The XStack subsystem enforcing compatibility and migration rules.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Compatibility}
The ability to maintain deterministic behavior across versions.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Conservation guarantee}
The requirement that physical and logical invariants are preserved across simulation tiers.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Contract}
A normative rule set defining allowed behaviors and invariants.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{ControlX}
The orchestration and planning subsystem of XStack.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Creative}
An ExperienceProfile representing expanded construction authority governed by LawProfile.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{D}

\paragraph{Debug}
An ExperienceProfile or entitlement allowing diagnostic access.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Debug panel}
A non-\allowbreak{}diegetic interface enabled only under explicit LawProfile.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Deprecated}
A term or pattern forbidden for use in code identifiers.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Determinism}
The property that identical inputs produce identical state hashes.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Deterministic packaging}
Packaging process producing bitwise identical artifacts given identical inputs.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Derived artifact}
An artifact deterministically generated from canonical artifacts.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Dev}
Developer environment context.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Diegetic Lens}
A Lens existing within simulation ontology and accessible to Agents.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Diegetic UI}
A UI representation existing as in-\allowbreak{}world instrument or Assembly.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Distribution}
A packaged form of Binaries and Packs for release.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Domain}
A modular simulation subsystem representing a coherent phenomenon (e.\allowbreak{}g.\allowbreak{}, climate).\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Domain registry}
A canonical registry listing all active Domains.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Drift}
Deviation from Canon or structural invariants.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{E}

\paragraph{Editor}
An ExperienceProfile permitting scenario or blueprint modification.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Engine}
Domino, the deterministic universe simulation core (C17 mainline with C-\allowbreak{}compatible public ABI).\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Entitlement}
A permission token within AuthorityContext.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Epistemic scope}
The boundary of information accessible to an Agent.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Expand}
Increase simulation detail from Macro Capsule to Micro-\allowbreak{}simulation.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Execution plan}
A deterministic sequence of verification or simulation actions.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Execution Profile}
FAST, STRICT, or FULL verification profile.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{ExperienceProfile}
Defines presentation defaults, allowed lenses, and LawProfile bindings.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Extensible}
Capable of expansion via Domain packs without refactor.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{F}

\paragraph{Fake}
A representation not grounded in simulation ontology.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{FAST}
Incremental verification profile prioritizing speed.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Feature}
A declared addition conforming to Canon.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Fidelity}
Resolution level of solver approximation under conservation contract.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Fidelity Boundary}
The transition interface between solver tiers.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Fidelity policy}
Registry defining solver tier activation rules.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Field}
A deterministic property over space/\allowbreak{}time or Assembly.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{File}
A stored data or code unit within the repository.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Fixed-point math}
Deterministic arithmetic representation used by Engine.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Forwards compatible}
Ability to run older saves in newer versions with migration.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Forbidden}
Explicitly disallowed by Canon or RepoX.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Frame tick}
Presentation update cycle distinct from simulation tick.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Future proof}
Architecturally designed to allow extension without refactor.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{G}

\paragraph{Game}
Dominium, the C++17 gameplay layer atop Domino.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{GBN}
Global Build Number for release tracking.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Glossary}
This authoritative normative definition set.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Good}
Conforming to Canon and invariants.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{GUI}
Graphical User Interface.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{H}

\paragraph{Hardcore}
LawProfile with stricter constraints and no respawn.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{HUD}
Heads-\allowbreak{}up display; non-\allowbreak{}diegetic unless explicitly diegetic via instrument.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{I}

\paragraph{Identity}
Stable deterministic identifier for Universe or Assembly.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Identity fingerprint}
Canonical hash representing identity invariants.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Impact graph}
Dependency mapping from file changes to verification scope.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Instance}
A running SessionSpec execution context.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Interest radius}
Spatial boundary determining Micro-\allowbreak{}simulation activation.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Interest region}
Region under detailed simulation.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Invariant}
A rule that must always hold.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Issue}
Tracked deviation or defect.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{L}

\paragraph{Lab}
An ExperienceProfile for experimentation.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Law}
Constraint system governing Process execution.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{LawProfile}
Declarative rule set enabling/\allowbreak{}disabling Processes and lenses.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Lens}
Transformation from TruthModel to PerceivedModel.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{LOD}
Level of Detail; fidelity level in presentation or simulation.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{M}

\paragraph{Macro}
Aggregate simulation layer.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Macro Capsule}
Aggregate representation preserving invariants.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Macro-simulation}
High-\allowbreak{}level simulation of aggregates.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Merkle hash tree}
Content-\allowbreak{}addressed hashing system for subtree change detection.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Metric}
A quantitative measurement within simulation or verification.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Micro}
Detailed simulation layer.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Micro-simulation}
Fine-\allowbreak{}grained simulation of Assemblies and Fields.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{MissionSpec}
Declarative mission definition with predicates.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Mod}
Third-\allowbreak{}party Pack extending Domain or content.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Modular}
Composed of replaceable independent components.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{N}

\paragraph{Named RNG Stream}
Deterministic pseudo-\allowbreak{}random sequence identified by name.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Non-diegetic Lens}
Lens external to simulation ontology.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Non-diegetic UI}
UI not existing within ontology.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{O}

\paragraph{Observation artifact}
Deterministic output of Observation Kernel.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Observation Kernel}
Function mapping \texttt{TruthModel x Lens x LawProfile x AuthorityContext -\allowbreak{}> PerceivedModel}.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Official}
Pack signed and verified by SecureX.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Observer}
ExperienceProfile allowing non-\allowbreak{}mutating observation.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Overlay}
Presentation layer component rendered over scene.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{P}

\paragraph{Pack}
Modular content or Domain extension unit.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Package}
Bundled distribution artifact.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{ParameterBundle}
Numeric tuning configuration.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Parity}
Consistency across CLI, TUI, GUI.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{PerformX}
Performance enforcement subsystem.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Pipe dream}
Speculative future feature not yet implemented.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Platform}
Target operating environment.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Process}
The sole mutation mechanism.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Process-only mutation}
Invariant prohibiting mutation outside Process.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Profile}
Generic term referring to LawProfile or ExperienceProfile.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Program}
Executable binary.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Privilege level}
AuthorityContext permission tier.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{R}

\paragraph{Reality}
Simulation ontology truth.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Refusal}
Deterministic denial of Process execution.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Refusal Contract}
Normative structure requiring reason code and remediation hint.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Reliable}
Deterministic and invariant-\allowbreak{}preserving.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Renderer}
Presentation subsystem consuming PerceivedModel.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Replay}
Deterministic re-\allowbreak{}execution of Process log.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{RepoX}
Static governance enforcement subsystem.\allowbreak{}


\paragraph{Retro}
Legacy or historical pack context.\allowbreak{}

Normative invariant.\allowbreak{}

Security enforcement subsystem.\allowbreak{}
