\section{Foundation Lock}

\vonecallout{DomSlate}{Source}{\texttt{current} \texttt{human\_\allowbreak{}full\_\allowbreak{}text} \texttt{repo\_\allowbreak{}current} Source: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}repo/\allowbreak{}FOUNDATION\_\allowbreak{}LOCK.\allowbreak{}md}.\allowbreak{} Reason: current high-\allowbreak{}authority orientation source.\allowbreak{}}

\subsection{Foundation Lock}

Foundation Lock is the repository decision gate that determines whether Dominium can leave the Foundation Lock queue and begin a first narrow governed product slice.\allowbreak{}


Current closeout result: PASS\_\allowbreak{}WITH\_\allowbreak{}WARNINGS.\allowbreak{}


\texttt{FOUNDATION-\allowbreak{}CLOSEOUT-\allowbreak{}02} reran the Foundation Lock gate after \texttt{FOUNDATION-\allowbreak{}REPAIR-\allowbreak{}DEPENDENCY-\allowbreak{}DIRECTION-\allowbreak{}01} and closed the lock with warnings.\allowbreak{} \texttt{PORTABILITY-\allowbreak{}ARCH-\allowbreak{}POLICY-\allowbreak{}02} has since completed the first post-\allowbreak{}closeout hardening follow-\allowbreak{}up.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{What It Means}

Foundation Lock means the governance spine exists, validates in required scope, is documented, and is integrated with the normal fast strict proof gate.\allowbreak{} It allows only narrow product slices that obey the public surface, command, diagnostics, artifact, capability, provider, module, replacement, versioning, trust, and portability laws.\allowbreak{}


Foundation Lock does not mean full CTest is green, every compatibility corpus exists, every provider is implemented, every runtime trust rule is enforced, Workbench UI exists, or broad feature work is open.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{Required Layers}

\begin{itemize}
\item Fast strict test tier.\allowbreak{}
\item Public surface registry.\allowbreak{}
\item API/\allowbreak{}ABI canon.\allowbreak{}
\item Dependency direction law.\allowbreak{}
\item Command/\allowbreak{}refusal/\allowbreak{}result surface law.\allowbreak{}
\item Diagnostic and evidence registry.\allowbreak{}
\item Artifact identity law.\allowbreak{}
\item Schema/\allowbreak{}protocol evolution law.\allowbreak{}
\item Capability/\allowbreak{}refusal law.\allowbreak{}
\item Provider model.\allowbreak{}
\item Module/\allowbreak{}workspace/\allowbreak{}app composition law.\allowbreak{}
\item Replacement protocol.\allowbreak{}
\item Version/\allowbreak{}deprecation law.\allowbreak{}
\item Mod/\allowbreak{}pack trust model.\allowbreak{}
\item Portability matrix.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{Closeout Decision}

All required files for the 15 Foundation Lock layers are present.\allowbreak{}


\texttt{FOUNDATION-\allowbreak{}CLOSEOUT-\allowbreak{}01} was blocked because dependency-\allowbreak{}direction strict reported \texttt{358} violations and \texttt{38} warnings.\allowbreak{}


\texttt{FOUNDATION-\allowbreak{}REPAIR-\allowbreak{}DEPENDENCY-\allowbreak{}DIRECTION-\allowbreak{}01} reports dependency-\allowbreak{}direction strict PASS with \texttt{0} violations and \texttt{68} warnings.\allowbreak{}


\texttt{FOUNDATION-\allowbreak{}CLOSEOUT-\allowbreak{}02} reports:


\begin{itemize}
\item dependency-\allowbreak{}direction strict: PASS with \texttt{0} violations and \texttt{68} warnings.\allowbreak{}
\item Foundation validator matrix: PASS.\allowbreak{}
\item AIDE doctor/\allowbreak{}validate/\allowbreak{}test/\allowbreak{}selftest/\allowbreak{}tools/\allowbreak{}roots/\allowbreak{}repo: PASS.\allowbreak{}
\item RepoX STRICT: PASS with stale AuditX warning.\allowbreak{}
\item fast strict: PASS, \texttt{32} commands, \texttt{272.\allowbreak{}607} seconds.\allowbreak{}
\item CMake configure/\allowbreak{}build and smoke CTest: PASS through fast strict.\allowbreak{}
\item full CTest: T4/\allowbreak{}full-\allowbreak{}gate debt, not run.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

Foundation Lock is PASS\_\allowbreak{}WITH\_\allowbreak{}WARNINGS.\allowbreak{}


\texttt{PORTABILITY-\allowbreak{}ARCH-\allowbreak{}POLICY-\allowbreak{}02} reports:


\begin{itemize}
\item architecture policy validator: PASS.\allowbreak{}
\item portability matrix validator: PASS.\allowbreak{}
\item fast strict: PASS, \texttt{33} commands, \texttt{296.\allowbreak{}553} seconds.\allowbreak{}
\item CMake configure/\allowbreak{}build and smoke CTest: PASS through fast strict.\allowbreak{}
\item full CTest: T4/\allowbreak{}full-\allowbreak{}gate debt, not run.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{Allowed Work}

\begin{itemize}
\item Continue narrow governed product-\allowbreak{}spine slices recorded by \texttt{.\allowbreak{}aide/\allowbreak{}queue/\allowbreak{}current.\allowbreak{}toml}.\allowbreak{}
\item Run \texttt{AIDE-\allowbreak{}WORKFLOW-\allowbreak{}LAW-\allowbreak{}01} next if the queue remains reconciled after
\end{itemize}
\texttt{PRODUCT-\allowbreak{}SPINE-\allowbreak{}REVIEW-\allowbreak{}01}.\allowbreak{}

\begin{itemize}
\item Run \texttt{POINTER-\allowbreak{}WIDTH-\allowbreak{}SERIALIZATION-\allowbreak{}AUDIT-\allowbreak{}01} only if the descriptive pointer-\allowbreak{}width inventory should be promoted into a focused audit.\allowbreak{}
\item Continue documentation and evidence updates that do not bypass Foundation laws.\allowbreak{}
\item Continue documentation and evidence updates that keep remaining warnings and full-\allowbreak{}gate debt visible.\allowbreak{}
\item Keep Queue B hardening planned but not a substitute for the blocker repair.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{Blocked Work}

\begin{itemize}
\item Broad feature work remains blocked.\allowbreak{}
\item Workbench UI, runtime module loading, provider runtime, package runtime, gameplay, renderer, native GUI, release publication, and broad rewrites remain blocked.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{Feature Rules After Lock}

When the lock eventually passes, future narrow slices must register public surfaces, expose typed commands, use diagnostic and refusal codes, preserve artifact identity, declare capabilities and providers, use module descriptors where applicable, and use the replacement protocol for rewrites.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{Authorized Narrow Product-Spine Slices}

\texttt{FOUNDATION-\allowbreak{}CLOSEOUT-\allowbreak{}02} authorized narrow product-\allowbreak{}spine work.\allowbreak{} Completed

narrow slices include \texttt{WORKBENCH-\allowbreak{}VALIDATION-\allowbreak{}SLICE-\allowbreak{}01},

\texttt{COMMAND-\allowbreak{}RESULT-\allowbreak{}VIEW-\allowbreak{}SLICE-\allowbreak{}01}, \texttt{PACKAGE-\allowbreak{}MOUNT-\allowbreak{}SLICE-\allowbreak{}01},

\texttt{REPLAY-\allowbreak{}PROOF-\allowbreak{}SLICE-\allowbreak{}01}, and \texttt{BAREBONES-\allowbreak{}CLIENT-\allowbreak{}SHELL-\allowbreak{}01}.\allowbreak{}


This authorization remains narrow.\allowbreak{} It does not authorize broad Workbench UI,

gameplay, renderer, native GUI, runtime provider expansion, package runtime,

release publication, or domain feature work.\allowbreak{}


Next recommended tasks:


\begin{enumerate}
\item \texttt{AIDE-\allowbreak{}WORKFLOW-\allowbreak{}LAW-\allowbreak{}01}
\item \texttt{PRESENTATION-\allowbreak{}CONTRACT-\allowbreak{}01}
\item \texttt{POINTER-\allowbreak{}WIDTH-\allowbreak{}SERIALIZATION-\allowbreak{}AUDIT-\allowbreak{}01}
\end{enumerate}



\section{What This Project Is (canon0)}

\vonecallout{DomSlate}{Source}{\texttt{current} \texttt{human\_\allowbreak{}full\_\allowbreak{}text} \texttt{architecture\_\allowbreak{}current} Source: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}WHAT\_\allowbreak{}THIS\_\allowbreak{}IS.\allowbreak{}md}.\allowbreak{} Reason: current high-\allowbreak{}authority orientation source.\allowbreak{}}

Future Series: DOC-\allowbreak{}ARCHIVE

Replacement Target: legacy reference surface retained without current binding authority


\subsection{What This Project Is (CANON0)}





Status: binding.\allowbreak{}



Scope: canonical statement of identity and intent.\allowbreak{}






Dominium/\allowbreak{}Domino is a deterministic world runtime and law-\allowbreak{}governed simulation OS.\allowbreak{}



It is built to host multi-\allowbreak{}scale universes with explicit existence, travel,



authority, and time perception.\allowbreak{}






\subsubsection{Core identity}


\begin{itemize}
\item A deterministic simulation runtime with reproducible outcomes.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item A truth/\allowbreak{}perception split where views are derived and authoritative state is
\end{itemize}


explicit.\allowbreak{}



\begin{itemize}
\item A law-\allowbreak{}governed simulation OS where authority is data-\allowbreak{}defined.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item A multi-\allowbreak{}scale reality model with explicit existence/\allowbreak{}refinement and visitability.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item A product stack (engine + game + client/\allowbreak{}server + launcher/\allowbreak{}setup + tools) that
\end{itemize}


separates runtime, control plane, and tooling.\allowbreak{}



\begin{itemize}
\item Content-\allowbreak{}agnostic executables: all meaning comes from packs resolved by UPS.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item Zero-\allowbreak{}asset boot paths for all products.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{It can host}


\begin{itemize}
\item player-\allowbreak{}only worlds
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item AI-\allowbreak{}only autorun universes
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item mixed civilizations
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item spectator museums and replays
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item anarchy servers
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item god-\allowbreak{}mode admin tools (law-\allowbreak{}gated and audited)
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{Invariants}


\begin{itemize}
\item Engine/\allowbreak{}game separation is preserved.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item Determinism and provenance are enforced.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item Absence and refusal are valid outcomes, not errors.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item There are no game modes; behavior is law + capability + policy.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{Forbidden assumptions}


\begin{itemize}
\item It is not acceptable to bypass law or audit for convenience.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item It is not acceptable to fabricate existence or resources.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{Dependencies}


\begin{itemize}
\item Canon and invariants: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}INVARIANTS.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item Reality layer: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}REALITY\_\allowbreak{}LAYER.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{See also}


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}CANONICAL\_\allowbreak{}SYSTEM\_\allowbreak{}MAP.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}INVARIANTS.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}REALITY\_\allowbreak{}MODEL.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}AUTHORITY\_\allowbreak{}MODEL.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}



\section{What This Project Is Not (canon0)}

\vonecallout{DomSlate}{Source}{\texttt{current} \texttt{human\_\allowbreak{}full\_\allowbreak{}text} \texttt{architecture\_\allowbreak{}current} Source: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}WHAT\_\allowbreak{}THIS\_\allowbreak{}IS\_\allowbreak{}NOT.\allowbreak{}md}.\allowbreak{} Reason: current high-\allowbreak{}authority orientation source.\allowbreak{}}

Future Series: DOC-\allowbreak{}CONVERGENCE

Replacement Target: canon-\allowbreak{}aligned documentation set for convergence and release preparation


\subsection{What This Project Is Not (CANON0)}





Status: binding.\allowbreak{}



Scope: guardrails against common misunderstandings.\allowbreak{}






\subsubsection{Not a traditional game engine}


It is not a generic rendering or physics framework; rendering is derived and



authoritative logic is deterministic and law-\allowbreak{}gated.\allowbreak{}






\subsubsection{Not an asset-dependent runtime}


Executables do not embed content; packs are external and optional.\allowbreak{}






\subsubsection{Not a step-everything sandbox}


No global scans or per-\allowbreak{}ACT AI loops; simulation advances via scheduled events.\allowbreak{}






\subsubsection{Not a physics-everywhere simulator}


Micro detail is refined only when required; macro existence is valid.\allowbreak{}






\subsubsection{Not a modes-based game}


There are no hard-\allowbreak{}coded modes; laws and capabilities define behavior.\allowbreak{}






\subsubsection{Not a cheat-based admin system}


Admin power is capability-\allowbreak{} and law-\allowbreak{}gated, audited, and fork-\allowbreak{}aware.\allowbreak{}






\subsubsection{Not a single-scale simulation}


It supports macro-\allowbreak{}only, meso, and micro refinement with explicit contracts.\allowbreak{}






\subsubsection{Invariants}


\begin{itemize}
\item Deterministic, law-\allowbreak{}gated authority is mandatory.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item Global iteration and implicit background simulation are forbidden.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item No hard-\allowbreak{}coded modes exist.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{Forbidden assumptions}


\begin{itemize}
\item "Convenient" implicit behavior is not allowed.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item Authority cannot bypass audit or law gates.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{Dependencies}


\begin{itemize}
\item Canon and invariants: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}INVARIANTS.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item Reality layer: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}REALITY\_\allowbreak{}LAYER.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{See also}


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}WHAT\_\allowbreak{}THIS\_\allowbreak{}IS.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}INVARIANTS.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}REALITY\_\allowbreak{}MODEL.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}AUTHORITY\_\allowbreak{}MODEL.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}



\section{Invariants (canon0)}

\vonecallout{DomSlate}{Source}{\texttt{current} \texttt{human\_\allowbreak{}full\_\allowbreak{}text} \texttt{architecture\_\allowbreak{}current} Source: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}INVARIANTS.\allowbreak{}md}.\allowbreak{} Reason: current high-\allowbreak{}authority orientation source.\allowbreak{}}

Future Series: DOC-\allowbreak{}CONVERGENCE

Replacement Target: canon-\allowbreak{}aligned documentation set for convergence and release preparation


\subsection{Invariants (CANON0)}





Status: binding.\allowbreak{}



Scope: hard invariants for all systems, documentation, and data.\allowbreak{}






Canonical summary: this document.\allowbreak{}






Each invariant includes why it exists, what breaks if violated, and which



systems enforce it.\allowbreak{}






\subsubsection{Invariant: Deterministic authoritative simulation (batch == step)}


Why:



\begin{itemize}
\item Reproducibility, auditability, and cross-\allowbreak{}platform agreement depend on it.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Breaks if violated:



\begin{itemize}
\item Replays diverge, cross-\allowbreak{}shard reconciliation fails, and saves become invalid.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Enforced by:



\begin{itemize}
\item Work IR + Access IR (\texttt{schema/\allowbreak{}execution/\allowbreak{}README.\allowbreak{}md})
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}EXECUTION\_\allowbreak{}REORDERING\_\allowbreak{}POLICY.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}DETERMINISTIC\_\allowbreak{}REDUCTION\_\allowbreak{}RULES.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item CI: EXEC0b-\allowbreak{}REORDER-\allowbreak{}001, EXEC0b-\allowbreak{}COMMIT-\allowbreak{}001
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{Invariant: Simulation advances only via explicit events (no global scans)}


Why:



\begin{itemize}
\item Event scheduling keeps costs bounded and deterministic.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Breaks if violated:



\begin{itemize}
\item Hidden background work, O(N) scans, and per-\allowbreak{}tick AI loops cause drift and
\end{itemize}


unpredictable budgets.\allowbreak{}



Enforced by:



\begin{itemize}
\item ARCH0 A2 (\texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}ARCH0\_\allowbreak{}CONSTITUTION.\allowbreak{}md})
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item Event-\allowbreak{}driven scheduling specs (e.\allowbreak{}g.\allowbreak{}, \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}reference/\allowbreak{}specs/\allowbreak{}SPEC\_\allowbreak{}EVENT\_\allowbreak{}DRIVEN\_\allowbreak{}STEPPING.\allowbreak{}md})
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item Guides: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}development/\allowbreak{}guides/\allowbreak{}NO\_\allowbreak{}GLOBAL\_\allowbreak{}ITERATION\_\allowbreak{}GUIDE.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item CI: CIV5-\allowbreak{}WAR3-\allowbreak{}NOGLOB-\allowbreak{}005, CIV5-\allowbreak{}WAR4-\allowbreak{}NOGLOB-\allowbreak{}004
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{Invariant: ACT is monotonic and never warped}


Why:



\begin{itemize}
\item ACT is the authoritative time axis for determinism and ordering.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Breaks if violated:



\begin{itemize}
\item Travel scheduling, replay, and law decisions become nondeterministic.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Enforced by:



\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}TIME\_\allowbreak{}DILATION\_\allowbreak{}WITHOUT\_\allowbreak{}TIME\_\allowbreak{}WARP.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{schema/\allowbreak{}time/\allowbreak{}README.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item CI: TIME2-\allowbreak{}NO-\allowbreak{}ACT-\allowbreak{}WARP-\allowbreak{}001
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{Invariant: No implicit existence}


Why:



\begin{itemize}
\item Existence must be auditable and lawful.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Breaks if violated:



\begin{itemize}
\item Pop-\allowbreak{}in creation, silent erasure, and unverifiable provenance.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Enforced by:



\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}EXISTENCE\_\allowbreak{}AND\_\allowbreak{}REALITY.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{schema/\allowbreak{}existence/\allowbreak{}README.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item CI: EXIST0-\allowbreak{}STATE-\allowbreak{}001, EXIST0-\allowbreak{}NOPOP-\allowbreak{}002
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{Invariant: No refinement without a contract}


Why:



\begin{itemize}
\item Refinement must be deterministic and provenance-\allowbreak{}preserving.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Breaks if violated:



\begin{itemize}
\item Fake worlds, fabricated history, and nondeterministic detail.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Enforced by:



\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}REFINEMENT\_\allowbreak{}CONTRACTS.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}VISITABILITY\_\allowbreak{}CONSISTENCY.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item CI: EXIST1-\allowbreak{}CONTRACT-\allowbreak{}001, DOMAIN4-\allowbreak{}NOFAKE-\allowbreak{}002
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{Invariant: No teleport without a TravelEdge}


Why:



\begin{itemize}
\item Movement must be schedulable, law-\allowbreak{}gated, and auditable.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Breaks if violated:



\begin{itemize}
\item Reachability lies, bypassed costs, and broken domain law.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Enforced by:



\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}TRAVEL\_\allowbreak{}AND\_\allowbreak{}MOVEMENT.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}NO\_\allowbreak{}MAGIC\_\allowbreak{}TELEPORTS.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item CI: TRAVEL0-\allowbreak{}NO-\allowbreak{}TELEPORT-\allowbreak{}001, TRAVEL2-\allowbreak{}NO-\allowbreak{}MAGIC-\allowbreak{}001
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{Invariant: Reachability implies visitability}


Why:



\begin{itemize}
\item If something can be reached, it must be real and refinable.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Breaks if violated:



\begin{itemize}
\item Players can arrive at non-\allowbreak{}real or non-\allowbreak{}refinable destinations.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Enforced by:



\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}VISITABILITY\_\allowbreak{}AND\_\allowbreak{}REALITY.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{schema/\allowbreak{}domain/\allowbreak{}SPEC\_\allowbreak{}VISITABILITY.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item CI: DOMAIN4-\allowbreak{}VISIT-\allowbreak{}001, DOMAIN4-\allowbreak{}NOFAKE-\allowbreak{}002
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{Invariant: No authority without capability and law}


Why:



\begin{itemize}
\item Authority must be explicit, scoped, and auditable.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Breaks if violated:



\begin{itemize}
\item Hidden admin bypass, cheat-\allowbreak{}only paths, and unverifiable outcomes.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Enforced by:



\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}AUTHORITY\_\allowbreak{}AND\_\allowbreak{}OMNIPOTENCE.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}LAW\_\allowbreak{}ENFORCEMENT\_\allowbreak{}POINTS.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{schema/\allowbreak{}authority/\allowbreak{}README.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item CI: OMNI0-\allowbreak{}NO-\allowbreak{}ISADMIN-\allowbreak{}001, OMNI0-\allowbreak{}NOBYPASS-\allowbreak{}003
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{Invariant: Authority gates actions only, never visibility (AUTH3-AUTH-001)}


Why:



\begin{itemize}
\item Visibility is epistemic; authority is action gating only.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Breaks if violated:



\begin{itemize}
\item Hidden enforcement, nondeterministic views, and un-\allowbreak{}auditable censorship.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Enforced by:



\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}AUTHORITY\_\allowbreak{}AND\_\allowbreak{}ENTITLEMENTS.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}DEMO\_\allowbreak{}AND\_\allowbreak{}TOURIST\_\allowbreak{}MODEL.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item Tests: \texttt{tests/\allowbreak{}authority/\allowbreak{}}, \texttt{tests/\allowbreak{}integration/\allowbreak{}tourist/\allowbreak{}}
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{Invariant: Entitlements gate authority issuance only (AUTH3-ENT-002)}


Why:



\begin{itemize}
\item Entitlements are platform-\allowbreak{}facing; engine/\allowbreak{}game must stay neutral.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Breaks if violated:



\begin{itemize}
\item Platform lock-\allowbreak{}in and hidden enforcement in simulation logic.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Enforced by:



\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}DISTRIBUTION\_\allowbreak{}AND\_\allowbreak{}STOREFRONTS.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item Tests: \texttt{tests/\allowbreak{}entitlement/\allowbreak{}}
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{Invariant: Demo is an authority profile, not a build (AUTH3-DEMO-003)}


Why:



\begin{itemize}
\item One distribution prevents paywalled forks and drift.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Breaks if violated:



\begin{itemize}
\item Divergent code paths and inconsistent determinism.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Enforced by:



\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}DISTRIBUTION\_\allowbreak{}AND\_\allowbreak{}STOREFRONTS.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}DEMO\_\allowbreak{}AND\_\allowbreak{}TOURIST\_\allowbreak{}MODEL.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item Tests: \texttt{tests/\allowbreak{}demo/\allowbreak{}}, \texttt{tests/\allowbreak{}distribution/\allowbreak{}}
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{Invariant: Tourists never mutate authoritative state (AUTH3-TOURIST-004)}


Why:



\begin{itemize}
\item Observation must not become hidden authority.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Breaks if violated:



\begin{itemize}
\item Untracked mutations and integrity drift.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Enforced by:



\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}DEMO\_\allowbreak{}AND\_\allowbreak{}TOURIST\_\allowbreak{}MODEL.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item Tests: \texttt{tests/\allowbreak{}integration/\allowbreak{}tourist/\allowbreak{}}
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{Invariant: Services affect access only (AUTH3-SERVICE-005)}


Why:



\begin{itemize}
\item Services are optional and external to determinism.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Breaks if violated:



\begin{itemize}
\item Altered outcomes and invalidated replays.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Enforced by:



\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}SERVICES\_\allowbreak{}AND\_\allowbreak{}PRODUCTS.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item Tests: \texttt{tests/\allowbreak{}contract/\allowbreak{}service/\allowbreak{}services\_\allowbreak{}expiry/\allowbreak{}}
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{Invariant: Piracy contained by authority, not DRM (AUTH3-PIRACY-006)}


Why:



\begin{itemize}
\item Copying is allowed; durable value is authority-\allowbreak{}bound.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Breaks if violated:



\begin{itemize}
\item Hidden penalties, degraded simulation, and non-\allowbreak{}archival behavior.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Enforced by:



\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}PIRACY\_\allowbreak{}CONTAINMENT.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item Tests: \texttt{tests/\allowbreak{}piracy\_\allowbreak{}containment/\allowbreak{}}
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{Invariant: Authority upgrades/downgrades do not mutate state (AUTH3-UPGRADE-007)}


Why:



\begin{itemize}
\item Authority changes are administrative, not simulation events.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Breaks if violated:



\begin{itemize}
\item Hidden state mutation and replay divergence.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Enforced by:



\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}UPGRADE\_\allowbreak{}AND\_\allowbreak{}CONVERSION.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item Tests: \texttt{tests/\allowbreak{}authority/\allowbreak{}}, \texttt{tests/\allowbreak{}contract/\allowbreak{}service/\allowbreak{}services\_\allowbreak{}expiry/\allowbreak{}}
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{Invariant: Saves are tagged by authority scope (AUTH3-SAVE-008)}


Why:



\begin{itemize}
\item Save provenance must remain explicit and auditable.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Breaks if violated:



\begin{itemize}
\item Silent promotion of non-\allowbreak{}authoritative saves.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Enforced by:



\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}UPGRADE\_\allowbreak{}AND\_\allowbreak{}CONVERSION.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item Tests: \texttt{tests/\allowbreak{}authority/\allowbreak{}}
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{Invariant: Control layers never interfere with authoritative simulation}


Why:



\begin{itemize}
\item Control layers are optional and external; they must not change outcomes.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Breaks if violated:



\begin{itemize}
\item Replays diverge, archival verification fails, and law enforcement becomes
\end{itemize}


untrustworthy.\allowbreak{}



Enforced by:



\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}NON\_\allowbreak{}INTERFERENCE.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}CONTROL\_\allowbreak{}LAYERS.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item Tests: \texttt{tests/\allowbreak{}runtime/\allowbreak{}control/\allowbreak{}interference/\allowbreak{}}
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{Invariant: No secrets in engine or game}


Why:



\begin{itemize}
\item Engine/\allowbreak{}game are portable, public, and replay-\allowbreak{}verifiable; secrets break trust.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Breaks if violated:



\begin{itemize}
\item Credential exposure, covert policy enforcement, and irreproducible builds.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Enforced by:



\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}CONTROL\_\allowbreak{}LAYERS.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}THREAT\_\allowbreak{}MODEL.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item Tests: \texttt{tests/\allowbreak{}runtime/\allowbreak{}control/\allowbreak{}audit/\allowbreak{}}
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{Invariant: Refusal and absence are first-class outcomes}


Why:



\begin{itemize}
\item Systems must fail deterministically and explainably.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Breaks if violated:



\begin{itemize}
\item Silent fallbacks, undefined behavior, or forced workarounds.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


Enforced by:



\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}REFUSAL\_\allowbreak{}AND\_\allowbreak{}EXPLANATION\_\allowbreak{}MODEL.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item ARCH0 A7 (\texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}ARCH0\_\allowbreak{}CONSTITUTION.\allowbreak{}md})
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item CI: EXEC0-\allowbreak{}ABSENCE-\allowbreak{}001
\end{itemize}

\begin{itemize}

\section{Canonical System Map (canon0)}

\vonecallout{DomSlate}{Source}{\texttt{current} \texttt{human\_\allowbreak{}full\_\allowbreak{}text} \texttt{architecture\_\allowbreak{}current} Source: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}CANONICAL\_\allowbreak{}SYSTEM\_\allowbreak{}MAP.\allowbreak{}md}.\allowbreak{} Reason: current high-\allowbreak{}authority orientation source.\allowbreak{}}

Future Series: DOC-\allowbreak{}CONVERGENCE

Replacement Target: canon-\allowbreak{}aligned documentation set for convergence and release preparation


\subsection{Canonical System Map (CANON0)}





Status: binding.\allowbreak{}



Scope: single-\allowbreak{}source dependency map and forbidden edges for Dominium/\allowbreak{}Domino.\allowbreak{}






This map locks the project into one mental model.\allowbreak{} It is written for humans and



is the authoritative dependency direction statement.\allowbreak{} "A -\allowbreak{}> B" means A depends



on B and must not be inverted.\allowbreak{}






\subsubsection{Canonical system stack (textual diagram)}


This stack is a navigation and integration view.\allowbreak{} Dependency direction remains



authoritative in the sections below.\allowbreak{}






ENGINE -\allowbreak{}> GAME -\allowbreak{}> SERVER/\allowbreak{}CLIENT -\allowbreak{}> LAUNCHER/\allowbreak{}SETUP -\allowbreak{}> TOOLS






\subsubsection{Invariants}


\begin{itemize}
\item Dependency direction is authoritative and must not be inverted.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item Engine and game responsibilities remain separated.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item Law gates and audit are mandatory for authoritative effects.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item Engine and game are content-\allowbreak{}agnostic executables; content lives in data.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item Launcher and setup are orchestration surfaces only.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item Tools are read-\allowbreak{}only by default and mutate state only via ToolIntents.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{Responsibilities and forbidden dependencies (quick map)}


Responsibilities:



\begin{itemize}
\item engine: mechanisms, determinism, storage, execution substrate, law gates
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item game: meaning, rules, process emission, law targets, content interpretation
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item server/\allowbreak{}client: product shells that compose engine + game
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item launcher/\allowbreak{}setup: orchestration, installation, profiles, compatibility
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item tools: validation, inspection, authoring, and audit-\allowbreak{}friendly workflows
\end{itemize}





Forbidden dependencies (summary):



\begin{itemize}
\item engine -\allowbreak{}> game, launcher, setup, tools, libs contracts
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item game -\allowbreak{}> launcher, setup, tools, libs contracts
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item launcher/\allowbreak{}setup/\allowbreak{}tools -\allowbreak{}> game rule mutation paths
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item client/\allowbreak{}server -\allowbreak{}> launcher, setup, tools
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item tools -\allowbreak{}> authoritative mutation outside ToolIntents
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{1) Engine vs Game Boundary}


Engine defines mechanisms; game defines meaning; data defines configuration.\allowbreak{}



Tools are read-\allowbreak{}only observers unless they emit explicit ToolIntents that are



law-\allowbreak{}gated and audited.\allowbreak{}






Dependency direction:



ENGINE: platform + syscaps -\allowbreak{}> execution substrate -\allowbreak{}> ECS storage -\allowbreak{}> world services



(domains, travel, time, law gates)



GAME: rules -\allowbreak{}> intents -\allowbreak{}> Work IR -\allowbreak{}> engine execution substrate



PRODUCTS: client/\allowbreak{}server -\allowbreak{}> engine + game



CONTROL PLANE: launcher/\allowbreak{}setup -\allowbreak{}> libs/\allowbreak{}contracts



TOOLS: tools -\allowbreak{}> libs/\allowbreak{}contracts (+ engine public API only, read-\allowbreak{}only)



SCHEMA: schema -\allowbreak{}> data formats only (no runtime logic)






Forbidden dependencies:



\begin{itemize}
\item engine -\allowbreak{}> game/\allowbreak{}launcher/\allowbreak{}setup/\allowbreak{}tools/\allowbreak{}libs
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item game -\allowbreak{}> launcher/\allowbreak{}setup/\allowbreak{}tools/\allowbreak{}libs
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item launcher/\allowbreak{}setup/\allowbreak{}tools -\allowbreak{}> game (no rule mutation)
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item client/\allowbreak{}server -\allowbreak{}> tools/\allowbreak{}package/\allowbreak{}launcher/\allowbreak{}setup
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item tools -\allowbreak{}> authoritative mutation outside ToolIntents
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{2) Execution Substrate}


All authoritative work is expressed as Work IR with Access IR declarations.\allowbreak{}



Law admission gates sit before scheduling, before execution, and before commit.\allowbreak{}






Dependency direction:



game systems -\allowbreak{}> Work IR + Access IR -\allowbreak{}> scheduler backends -\allowbreak{}> deterministic commit



law kernel -\allowbreak{}> admission gates -\allowbreak{}> task/\allowbreak{}effect execution



budgets + SysCaps -\allowbreak{}> execution policy -\allowbreak{}> backend selection






Forbidden dependencies:



\begin{itemize}
\item gameplay code bypassing Work IR or spawning threads
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item derived/\allowbreak{}presentation tasks writing authoritative state
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item scheduler policy encoded inside game rules
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{3) Storage (ECS)}


ECS schemas define component meaning; storage layout is an engine backend choice.\allowbreak{}



Game code depends on logical components, not layout or memory order.\allowbreak{}






Dependency direction:



schema/\allowbreak{}ecs -\allowbreak{}> engine storage -\allowbreak{}> game rules -\allowbreak{}> Work IR tasks






Forbidden dependencies:



\begin{itemize}
\item gameplay logic depending on physical storage layout
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item storage backends altering component semantics or determinism
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{4) Space \& Domains}
Domain volumes define where reality exists and which laws apply.\allowbreak{} Domain queries

are deterministic, budgeted, and SDF-\allowbreak{}based.\allowbreak{}


Dependency direction:

domain volumes -\allowbreak{}> reachability + law jurisdictions -\allowbreak{}> travel + refinement


Forbidden dependencies:

\begin{itemize}
\item implicit world bounds or rectangular assumptions
\item domain checks bypassing domain query API
\end{itemize}

Terrain truth (TERRAIN0) is field-\allowbreak{}defined and provider-\allowbreak{}resolved.\allowbreak{}


Dependency direction:

domain volumes -\allowbreak{}> terrain field stack -\allowbreak{}> provider chain -\allowbreak{}> overlays -\allowbreak{}> queries


Forbidden dependencies:

\begin{itemize}
\item meshes treated as authoritative truth
\item per-\allowbreak{}tick global erosion
\item planet/\allowbreak{}station special casing in terrain truth
\end{itemize}



\subsubsection{5) Existence \& Refinement}


Existence states are explicit; transitions are effects.\allowbreak{} Refinement contracts



deterministically realize micro state; collapse preserves truth and provenance.\allowbreak{}






Dependency direction:



existence state -\allowbreak{}> refinement contract -\allowbreak{}> visitability -\allowbreak{}> travel arrival



law kernel + Work IR -\allowbreak{}> existence transitions






Forbidden dependencies:



\begin{itemize}
\item implicit existence creation/\allowbreak{}destruction
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item refinement without a contract
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item history edits without archival fork
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{6) Travel \& Reachability}


All movement is scheduled travel over explicit edges with cost/\allowbreak{}capacity rules.\allowbreak{}



Visitability gates arrival.\allowbreak{}






Dependency direction:



travel graph -\allowbreak{}> ACT scheduling -\allowbreak{}> law/\allowbreak{}capability checks -\allowbreak{}> arrival effects



domain permissions + existence/\allowbreak{}refinement -\allowbreak{}> visitability decision






Forbidden dependencies:



\begin{itemize}
\item teleportation without a TravelEdge
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item arrival into non-\allowbreak{}refinable or archived targets
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item bypassing law or visitability gates
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{7) Time \& Perception}


ACT is authoritative and monotonic.\allowbreak{} Observer clocks derive perception without



changing schedules.\allowbreak{} Replay uses the same model.\allowbreak{}






Dependency direction:



ACT -\allowbreak{}> scheduler -\allowbreak{}> authoritative effects



observer clocks -\allowbreak{}> presentation/\allowbreak{}replay views






Forbidden dependencies:



\begin{itemize}
\item ACT warping for gameplay pacing
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item perception clocks affecting authoritative scheduling
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item future leakage beyond allowed buffers
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{8) Authority, Law \& Integrity}


Capabilities grant power; laws decide outcomes; policy constrains behavior.\allowbreak{}



Integrity signals inform law but never mutate state.\allowbreak{}






Dependency direction:



capabilities + law targets + policy -\allowbreak{}> law kernel -\allowbreak{}> accept/\allowbreak{}refuse/\allowbreak{}transform



law outcomes -\allowbreak{}> effects + audit + refusal explanations






Forbidden dependencies:



\begin{itemize}
\item isAdmin/\allowbreak{}mode checks in code
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item admin/\allowbreak{}cheat bypass without law + audit
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item silent fallbacks in the face of denial
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{9) Distribution \& Sharding}


Shard ownership is deterministic and domain-\allowbreak{}driven.\allowbreak{} Cross-\allowbreak{}shard messages are



ordered deterministically; no synchronous cross-\allowbreak{}shard reads.\allowbreak{}






Dependency direction:



domain partition -\allowbreak{}> shard ownership -\allowbreak{}> message ordering -\allowbreak{}> commit






Forbidden dependencies:



\begin{itemize}
\item nondeterministic shard placement
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item state teleportation or silent migration
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item synchronous cross-\allowbreak{}shard reads
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{10) Tooling \& Omnipotence}


Tooling is capability-\allowbreak{}gated.\allowbreak{} Omnipotence is the union of capabilities and is



still law-\allowbreak{}gated, audited, and constrained by archival rules.\allowbreak{}






Dependency direction:



ToolIntents -\allowbreak{}> law kernel -\allowbreak{}> effects -\allowbreak{}> audit



omnipotent intent -\allowbreak{}> same path






Forbidden dependencies:



\begin{itemize}
\item tool-\allowbreak{}side mutation outside ToolIntents
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item history edits without archival fork + audit
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item bypassing law or integrity gates
\end{itemize}





\subsubsection{Forbidden assumptions}


\begin{itemize}
\item Dependency inversion is acceptable for convenience.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}


\begin{itemize}
\item Tooling can mutate authoritative state directly.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\section{Contracts Index (const0)}

\vonecallout{DomSlate}{Source}{\texttt{current} \texttt{human\_\allowbreak{}full\_\allowbreak{}text} \texttt{architecture\_\allowbreak{}current} Source: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}CONTRACTS\_\allowbreak{}INDEX.\allowbreak{}md}.\allowbreak{} Reason: current high-\allowbreak{}authority orientation source.\allowbreak{}}

Future Series: DOC-\allowbreak{}CONVERGENCE

Replacement Target: canon-\allowbreak{}aligned documentation set for convergence and release preparation


\subsection{Contracts Index (CONST0)}





Status: binding.\allowbreak{}



Scope: index of frozen and evolving constitutional surfaces.\allowbreak{}






This index is the navigation hub for stability surfaces.\allowbreak{} "FROZEN" means the



document defines a contract that must not change lightly.\allowbreak{} "EVOLVING" means the



document is binding but still expected to grow or sharpen.\allowbreak{}

\section{DOCS Current Project Picture}

\vonecallout{DomSlate}{Source}{\texttt{advisory} \texttt{human\_\allowbreak{}full\_\allowbreak{}text} \texttt{advisory\_\allowbreak{}synthesis} Source: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}archive/\allowbreak{}docs\_\allowbreak{}corpus/\allowbreak{}\_\allowbreak{}reconciliation/\allowbreak{}DOCS\_\allowbreak{}CURRENT\_\allowbreak{}PROJECT\_\allowbreak{}PICTURE\_\allowbreak{}v0.\allowbreak{}md}.\allowbreak{} Reason: required synthesis source.\allowbreak{}}

\subsection{Docs Current Project Picture}

Dominium's current documentation picture is authority layered.\allowbreak{} Canon, glossary, \texttt{AGENTS.\allowbreak{}md}, contract/\allowbreak{}schema law, current queue state, and validated repo artifacts are the highest-\allowbreak{}confidence sources.\allowbreak{} Archive and conversation material can explain how earlier ideas developed, but it cannot become current truth through this docs-\allowbreak{}corpus task.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{Current Orientation}

\begin{itemize}
\item Project orientation: \texttt{README.\allowbreak{}md}
\item Documentation taxonomy: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}README.\allowbreak{}md}
\item Canon: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}canon/\allowbreak{}constitution\_\allowbreak{}v1.\allowbreak{}md}
\item Glossary: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}canon/\allowbreak{}glossary\_\allowbreak{}v1.\allowbreak{}md}
\item Agent governance: \texttt{AGENTS.\allowbreak{}md}
\item Queue state: \texttt{.\allowbreak{}aide/\allowbreak{}queue/\allowbreak{}current.\allowbreak{}toml}
\item Foundation status: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}repo/\allowbreak{}FOUNDATION\_\allowbreak{}LOCK.\allowbreak{}md}
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{Corpus Scale}

\begin{itemize}
\item Files represented: 5116
\item Markdown files: 4671
\item Archive/\allowbreak{}conversation files: 3221
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{What Is Safe To Do With This Output}

\begin{itemize}
\item Read the docs corpus as a map.\allowbreak{}
\item Use archive material for provenance and review.\allowbreak{}
\item Use generated contradictions and promotion queues to plan later tasks.\allowbreak{}
\item Start later live-\allowbreak{}doc patches only through explicit narrow promotion tasks.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{What This Output Does Not Do}

\begin{itemize}
\item It does not promote archive claims.\allowbreak{}
\item It does not rewrite canon, contracts, schema, implementation, release, or queue state.\allowbreak{}
\item It does not open blocked renderer, gameplay, provider runtime, package runtime, broad Workbench UI, native GUI, or release publication work.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}



\section{DOCS Decision Docket}

\vonecallout{DomSlate}{Source}{\texttt{advisory} \texttt{human\_\allowbreak{}full\_\allowbreak{}text} \texttt{advisory\_\allowbreak{}synthesis} Source: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}archive/\allowbreak{}docs\_\allowbreak{}corpus/\allowbreak{}\_\allowbreak{}reconciliation/\allowbreak{}DOCS\_\allowbreak{}DECISION\_\allowbreak{}DOCKET\_\allowbreak{}v0.\allowbreak{}md}.\allowbreak{} Reason: required synthesis source.\allowbreak{}}

\subsection{Docs Decision Docket}

Decision items are review prompts.\allowbreak{} The default disposition is defer unless a later explicit task opens the scope.\allowbreak{}

\section{DOCS Promotion Queue}

\vonecallout{DomSlate}{Source}{\texttt{advisory} \texttt{human\_\allowbreak{}full\_\allowbreak{}text} \texttt{advisory\_\allowbreak{}synthesis} Source: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}archive/\allowbreak{}docs\_\allowbreak{}corpus/\allowbreak{}\_\allowbreak{}reconciliation/\allowbreak{}DOCS\_\allowbreak{}PROMOTION\_\allowbreak{}QUEUE\_\allowbreak{}v0.\allowbreak{}md}.\allowbreak{} Reason: required synthesis source.\allowbreak{}}

\section{Current Project Atlas V0}

\vonecallout{DomSlate}{Source}{\texttt{advisory} \texttt{human\_\allowbreak{}full\_\allowbreak{}text} \texttt{derived\_\allowbreak{}synthesis} Source: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}archive/\allowbreak{}conversations/\allowbreak{}\_\allowbreak{}synthesis/\allowbreak{}CURRENT\_\allowbreak{}PROJECT\_\allowbreak{}ATLAS\_\allowbreak{}v0.\allowbreak{}md}.\allowbreak{} Reason: derived synthesis/\allowbreak{}report used as readable source.\allowbreak{}}

Source Class: conversation\_\allowbreak{}corpus\_\allowbreak{}synthesis



\subsection{Current Project Atlas v0}

This atlas is a reader map.\allowbreak{} It is not canon and does not promote archived conversation claims.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{Read Order}

\begin{enumerate}
\item \href{../../../../README.md}{\uline{README.md}} for current project orientation.\allowbreak{}
\item \href{../../../canon/constitution_v1.md}{\uline{constitution\_v1.md}} and \href{../../../canon/glossary_v1.md}{\uline{glossary\_v1.md}} for binding meaning.\allowbreak{}
\item \href{../../../../AGENTS.md}{\uline{AGENTS.md}} and \href{../../../planning/AUTHORITY_ORDER.md}{\uline{AUTHORITY\_ORDER.md}} for repo/\allowbreak{}agent authority rules.\allowbreak{}
\item \href{../../../../.aide/queue/current.toml}{\uline{.aide/queue/current.toml}} for current scope gates.\allowbreak{}
\item \href{../_decision/DECISION_DOCKET_v0.md}{\uline{DECISION\_DOCKET\_v0.md}} and \href{../_promotion/PROMOTION_REVIEW_BOARD_v0.md}{\uline{PROMOTION\_REVIEW\_BOARD\_v0.md}} for archive-\allowbreak{}derived adjudication.\allowbreak{}
\end{enumerate}

\subsubsection{What Dominium Is}

Current repo truth: Dominium is a deterministic, contract-\allowbreak{}governed simulation game and operating environment built on the Domino deterministic substrate.\allowbreak{} It is about lawful simulation of invention, production, logistics, economics, settlement, trust, communication, and institutional power.\allowbreak{}


Conversation-\allowbreak{}derived context: the archive expands that picture into a long-\allowbreak{}horizon product ecosystem: engine substrate, official game/\allowbreak{}domain layer, Workbench, setup/\allowbreak{}launcher, content packs, portability, release identity, and repo-\allowbreak{}governed assistant workflows.\allowbreak{} That context is historical and advisory.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{What Domino Is}

Domino is the reusable deterministic substrate: execution ordering, storage, replay, ABI-\allowbreak{}facing boundaries, and engine mechanisms.\allowbreak{} Archived conversations consistently treat Domino as reusable infrastructure rather than a one-\allowbreak{}off game binary.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{Active Surfaces}

\begin{center}
{\small\renewcommand{\arraystretch}{1.18}
\begin{tabularx}{\linewidth}{@{}>{\raggedright\arraybackslash}X >{\raggedright\arraybackslash}X >{\raggedright\arraybackslash}X@{}}
\toprule
\textbf{Surface} & \textbf{Current Meaning} & \textbf{Archive Context} \\
\midrule
\texttt{engine/\allowbreak{}} & deterministic substrate & reusable Domino foundation \\
\texttt{game/\allowbreak{}} & Dominium domain rules and interpretation & official game/\allowbreak{}product layer \\
\texttt{runtime/\allowbreak{}} & shell/\allowbreak{}platform/\allowbreak{}adapters/\allowbreak{}diagnostics/\allowbreak{}storage host integration & platform and projection glue, not truth owner \\
\texttt{apps/\allowbreak{}} & thin product composition & client/\allowbreak{}server/\allowbreak{}launcher/\allowbreak{}setup/\allowbreak{}workbench entrypoints \\
\texttt{contracts/\allowbreak{}} and \texttt{schema/\allowbreak{}} & machine-\allowbreak{}readable law and compatibility meaning & promotion candidates need high review \\
\texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}archive/\allowbreak{}conversations/\allowbreak{}} & derived conversation evidence & source layer for synthesis, not authority \\
\texttt{tools/\allowbreak{}} & validators and repo tooling & repeatable audit/\allowbreak{}generation/\allowbreak{}control surfaces \\
\bottomrule
\end{tabularx}
}
\end{center}

\subsubsection{What Requires Review Before Promotion}

\begin{itemize}
\item Any claim touching canon, glossary, authority order, contracts, schema law, current queue, release, implementation, or blocked scope.\allowbreak{}
\item Any old language/\allowbreak{}platform/\allowbreak{}baseline claim.\allowbreak{}
\item Any claim whose target path is only a wildcard such as \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}architecture/\allowbreak{}**} or \texttt{contracts/\allowbreak{}**}.\allowbreak{}
\item Any Wave 1 candidate before source text and target docs are inspected together.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{Recommended Next Steps}

\begin{enumerate}
\item Manually review the decision docket and choose defer/\allowbreak{}preserve/\allowbreak{}promote-\allowbreak{}later dispositions.\allowbreak{}
\item Select a small subset of Wave 1 candidates for docs-\allowbreak{}only microtasks.\allowbreak{}
\item For each microtask, name the source claim ID, exact target doc, authority support, non-\allowbreak{}goals, validation, and promotion status update.\allowbreak{}
\item Keep implementation blocked unless the current queue opens it.\allowbreak{}
\end{enumerate}



\section{Dominium Conversation Corpus Synthesis Book V0}

\vonecallout{DomSlate}{Source}{\texttt{advisory} \texttt{human\_\allowbreak{}full\_\allowbreak{}text} \texttt{derived\_\allowbreak{}synthesis} Source: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}archive/\allowbreak{}conversations/\allowbreak{}\_\allowbreak{}synthesis/\allowbreak{}PROJECT\_\allowbreak{}SYNTHESIS\_\allowbreak{}BOOK\_\allowbreak{}v0.\allowbreak{}md}.\allowbreak{} Reason: derived synthesis/\allowbreak{}report used as readable source.\allowbreak{}}

Source Class: conversation\_\allowbreak{}corpus\_\allowbreak{}synthesis



\subsection{Dominium Conversation Corpus Synthesis Book v0}

This book is a derived reading guide over the archived conversation corpus.\allowbreak{} It is not canon, not architecture doctrine, not a contract, and not an implementation plan.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{1. Status And Authority}

\begin{itemize}
\item Acceptance review result: \texttt{PASS\_\allowbreak{}WITH\_\allowbreak{}WARNINGS}.\allowbreak{}
\item Authority class: \texttt{advisory\_\allowbreak{}synthesis}.\allowbreak{}
\item Promotion status: \texttt{not\_\allowbreak{}promoted}.\allowbreak{}
\item Current repo artifacts outrank every conversation-\allowbreak{}derived statement in this book.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{2. Executive Overview}

The archive describes Dominium as a long-\allowbreak{}horizon deterministic simulation product: a game, engine-\allowbreak{}backed operating environment, validation workbench, content platform, and governance-\allowbreak{}heavy repository.\allowbreak{} Across the conversations, the recurring intent is not to build a renderer-\allowbreak{}owned game loop or a pile of UI screens.\allowbreak{} The recurring intent is to preserve lawful simulation truth, expose it through command/\allowbreak{}result/\allowbreak{}evidence surfaces, and let products project that truth without mutating it.\allowbreak{}


The current repo already establishes the strongest version of that principle through canon, glossary, README, and queue state.\allowbreak{} The conversation corpus adds historical design intent around world scale, Workbench, setup/\allowbreak{}launcher, release identity, provider/\allowbreak{}content boundaries, and future UI/\allowbreak{}editor experiences.\allowbreak{} Those claims remain advisory until reconciled and promoted.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{3. What Dominium Is Trying To Be}

Repo-\allowbreak{}established truth: Dominium is the official game/\allowbreak{}product/\allowbreak{}domain layer on top of Domino, the reusable deterministic substrate.\allowbreak{} It is concerned with invention, production, logistics, economics, settlement, trust, communication, and institutional power emerging from lawful simulation.\allowbreak{}


Conversation-\allowbreak{}derived intent: the archive repeatedly extends that picture toward a broad universe-\allowbreak{}scale simulation platform, with real-\allowbreak{}world defaults, arbitrary authored packs, robust tooling, deterministic evidence, long-\allowbreak{}term portability, and a Workbench that makes the project inspectable and operable.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{4. Core Mental Model}

The current README gives the clearest spine: intent -\allowbreak{}> command -\allowbreak{}> capability/\allowbreak{}refusal check -\allowbreak{}> service or deterministic process -\allowbreak{}> result/\allowbreak{}document/\allowbreak{}snapshot -\allowbreak{}> diagnostics/\allowbreak{}evidence -\allowbreak{}> view/\allowbreak{}action model -\allowbreak{}> projection -\allowbreak{}> shell.\allowbreak{} The conversations mostly orbit that same model, even when they discuss UI, renderer, platform, setup, or release packaging.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{5. Engine / Game / Runtime / Product Boundaries}

Repo truth keeps Engine, Game, Client, Server, Workbench, setup, launcher, tools, contracts, and content in separate roles.\allowbreak{} Conversation-\allowbreak{}derived material reinforces the boundary: renderer and UI project state, clients issue intents, server/\allowbreak{}game/\allowbreak{}engine law remains authoritative, and tools validate or inspect rather than silently mutate truth.\allowbreak{}


Representative sources: \href{../_reader/by_chat/advanced_simulation_infrastructure.md}{\uline{Dominium Advanced Simulation and Infrastructure Architecture}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/app_runtime_platform_renderers.md}{\uline{Dominium APP0 Runtime, Platform, and Renderer Architecture}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/app_testx_codehygiene.md}{\uline{Dominium Architecture, Application Layer, TestX, and CodeHygiene Planning}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/architecture_codex_prompts.md}{\uline{Dominium/Domino Architecture and Codex Prompt Roadmap}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/architecture_ui_providers.md}{\uline{Dominium Architecture, UI, Providers, and Robot OS Strategy}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/build_and_future_proofing.md}{\uline{Dominium Build and Future-Proofing Architecture}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/canonical_structure_and_framework.md}{\uline{Dominium Canonical Architecture, Repository Foundation, and Provider Model}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/chronology_celestial_systems.md}{\uline{Dominium Chronology \& Celestial Systems}}.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{6. Determinism, Replay, And Provenance}

The canon makes determinism primary: ordering, reductions, RNG streams, replay, hash partitions, and provenance are non-\allowbreak{}negotiable.\allowbreak{} The corpus adds historical emphasis on deterministic world scale, portable builds, replay proofs, verification artifacts, and avoiding hidden fallback behavior.\allowbreak{}


Representative sources: \href{../_reader/by_chat/advanced_simulation_infrastructure.md}{\uline{Dominium Advanced Simulation and Infrastructure Architecture}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/app_runtime_platform_renderers.md}{\uline{Dominium APP0 Runtime, Platform, and Renderer Architecture}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/app_testx_codehygiene.md}{\uline{Dominium Architecture, Application Layer, TestX, and CodeHygiene Planning}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/architecture_codex_prompts.md}{\uline{Dominium/Domino Architecture and Codex Prompt Roadmap}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/architecture_ui_providers.md}{\uline{Dominium Architecture, UI, Providers, and Robot OS Strategy}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/build_and_future_proofing.md}{\uline{Dominium Build and Future-Proofing Architecture}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/canonical_structure_and_framework.md}{\uline{Dominium Canonical Architecture, Repository Foundation, and Provider Model}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/development_routes.md}{\uline{Dominium Development Routes and Continuity Preservation}}.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{7. Law, Authority, Refusal, And Capability Model}

Current repo truth says authority permits attempts, law decides accept/\allowbreak{}refuse/\allowbreak{}transform, and refusals must be deterministic and auditable.\allowbreak{} Conversations often use different local language, but the recurring direction is aligned: no convenience bypass, no generated output as truth, and no old prompt as authority.\allowbreak{}


Representative sources: \href{../_reader/by_chat/advanced_simulation_infrastructure.md}{\uline{Dominium Advanced Simulation and Infrastructure Architecture}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/app_runtime_platform_renderers.md}{\uline{Dominium APP0 Runtime, Platform, and Renderer Architecture}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/app_testx_codehygiene.md}{\uline{Dominium Architecture, Application Layer, TestX, and CodeHygiene Planning}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/architecture_codex_prompts.md}{\uline{Dominium/Domino Architecture and Codex Prompt Roadmap}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/architecture_ui_providers.md}{\uline{Dominium Architecture, UI, Providers, and Robot OS Strategy}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/build_and_future_proofing.md}{\uline{Dominium Build and Future-Proofing Architecture}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/canonical_structure_and_framework.md}{\uline{Dominium Canonical Architecture, Repository Foundation, and Provider Model}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/chronology_celestial_systems.md}{\uline{Dominium Chronology \& Celestial Systems}}.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{8. World, Reality, Scale, And Refinement Model}

Conversation-\allowbreak{}derived intent is expansive: worlds, planets, celestial systems, universe explorer concepts, chronology, spatial refinement, simulation domains, macro/\allowbreak{}micro transitions, and real-\allowbreak{}world defaults recur across the archive.\allowbreak{} This is a design-\allowbreak{}intent signal, not current implementation authority.\allowbreak{}


Representative sources: \href{../_reader/by_chat/app_runtime_platform_renderers.md}{\uline{Dominium APP0 Runtime, Platform, and Renderer Architecture}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/app_testx_codehygiene.md}{\uline{Dominium Architecture, Application Layer, TestX, and CodeHygiene Planning}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/architecture_codex_prompts.md}{\uline{Dominium/Domino Architecture and Codex Prompt Roadmap}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/architecture_ui_providers.md}{\uline{Dominium Architecture, UI, Providers, and Robot OS Strategy}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/build_and_future_proofing.md}{\uline{Dominium Build and Future-Proofing Architecture}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/chronology_celestial_systems.md}{\uline{Dominium Chronology \& Celestial Systems}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/development_routes.md}{\uline{Dominium Development Routes and Continuity Preservation}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/dominium_architecture_i.md}{\uline{Dominium Architecture I}}.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{9. Timekeeping, Chronology, And 2038 Resilience}

Time appears as both a simulation domain and a platform durability concern.\allowbreak{} The archive repeatedly points to chronology, calendars, celestial alignment, 2038 resilience, and timestamp policy.\allowbreak{} Current promotion must verify all such claims against current contracts and language/\allowbreak{}platform baselines.\allowbreak{}


Representative sources: \href{../_reader/by_chat/advanced_simulation_infrastructure.md}{\uline{Dominium Advanced Simulation and Infrastructure Architecture}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/app_runtime_platform_renderers.md}{\uline{Dominium APP0 Runtime, Platform, and Renderer Architecture}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/app_testx_codehygiene.md}{\uline{Dominium Architecture, Application Layer, TestX, and CodeHygiene Planning}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/architecture_codex_prompts.md}{\uline{Dominium/Domino Architecture and Codex Prompt Roadmap}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/canonical_structure_and_framework.md}{\uline{Dominium Canonical Architecture, Repository Foundation, and Provider Model}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/chronology_celestial_systems.md}{\uline{Dominium Chronology \& Celestial Systems}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/development_routes.md}{\uline{Dominium Development Routes and Continuity Preservation}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/documentation_standards_readme.md}{\uline{Documentation Standards, README Strategy, and Handoff Packaging}}.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{10. Civilization, Institutions, Economy, Logistics}

The corpus frames Dominium around emergent production, logistics, economics, settlement, communication, trust, institutions, and power.\allowbreak{} These are project identity themes; they are not authorization to open gameplay or runtime work while the current queue blocks it.\allowbreak{}


Representative sources: \href{../_reader/by_chat/advanced_simulation_infrastructure.md}{\uline{Dominium Advanced Simulation and Infrastructure Architecture}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/app_runtime_platform_renderers.md}{\uline{Dominium APP0 Runtime, Platform, and Renderer Architecture}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/app_testx_codehygiene.md}{\uline{Dominium Architecture, Application Layer, TestX, and CodeHygiene Planning}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/architecture_codex_prompts.md}{\uline{Dominium/Domino Architecture and Codex Prompt Roadmap}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/architecture_ui_providers.md}{\uline{Dominium Architecture, UI, Providers, and Robot OS Strategy}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/build_and_future_proofing.md}{\uline{Dominium Build and Future-Proofing Architecture}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/canonical_structure_and_framework.md}{\uline{Dominium Canonical Architecture, Repository Foundation, and Provider Model}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/chronology_celestial_systems.md}{\uline{Dominium Chronology \& Celestial Systems}}.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{11. UI, Renderer, Workbench, And Tools}

The conversations strongly prefer a rich Workbench and eventual editor/\allowbreak{}operator surfaces.\allowbreak{} Current authority is narrower: broad Workbench UI, renderer implementation, and native GUI remain blocked.\allowbreak{} Therefore synthesis may describe intent, but follow-\allowbreak{}up tasks must stay contract/\allowbreak{}planning scoped until the queue opens implementation scope.\allowbreak{}


Representative sources: \href{../_reader/by_chat/advanced_simulation_infrastructure.md}{\uline{Dominium Advanced Simulation and Infrastructure Architecture}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/architecture_ui_providers.md}{\uline{Dominium Architecture, UI, Providers, and Robot OS Strategy}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/canonical_structure_and_framework.md}{\uline{Dominium Canonical Architecture, Repository Foundation, and Provider Model}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/development_routes.md}{\uline{Dominium Development Routes and Continuity Preservation}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/dominium_architecture_iv.md}{\uline{Dominium Architecture IV}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/dominium_domino_codex_planning.md}{\uline{Dominium + Domino Codex Planning and Handoff}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/dominium_full_conversation.md}{\uline{Dominium Workbench, AIDE, Presentation Architecture, Provider Strategy, Product-Spine Planning, and Preservation Companion}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/domino_dominium_workbench.md}{\uline{Domino Dominium Workbench}}.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{12. AIDE, Codex, Governance, And Patch Workflow}

The archive treats AIDE/\allowbreak{}Codex/\allowbreak{}XStack as repo-\allowbreak{}control and patch-\allowbreak{}execution aids.\allowbreak{} Current repo truth agrees that they do not replace canon, contracts, review gates, or validation.\allowbreak{} Their correct role is bounded evidence-\allowbreak{}producing work, not direct semantic authority.\allowbreak{}


Representative sources: \href{../_reader/by_chat/app_testx_codehygiene.md}{\uline{Dominium Architecture, Application Layer, TestX, and CodeHygiene Planning}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/canonical_structure_and_framework.md}{\uline{Dominium Canonical Architecture, Repository Foundation, and Provider Model}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/dominium_complete_conversation.md}{\uline{Dominium Canon, Repository Alignment, and Portability Doctrine}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/dominium_full_conversation.md}{\uline{Dominium Workbench, AIDE, Presentation Architecture, Provider Strategy, Product-Spine Planning, and Preservation Companion}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/foundation_workbench_codex.md}{\uline{Dominium Foundation Lock, Workbench Spine, and Parallel Codex Handoff}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/language_platform_architecture.md}{\uline{Dominium Language, Platform, and Architecture Baseline}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/modularity_aide_refactorability.md}{\uline{Dominium Modularity, AIDE Refactorability, and Future-Proof Architecture}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/omega_xi_pi_architecture_future.md}{\uline{Dominium Omega/Xi/Pi Architecture \& Future-Proofing Planning}}.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{13. Release, Setup, Launcher, Platform, Portability}

Conversations cover setup, launcher, release identity, versioning, portability, platform support, and public distribution.\allowbreak{} Current queue still blocks release publication, so these remain planning and audit material unless a later reviewed task opens the scope.\allowbreak{}


Representative sources: \href{../_reader/by_chat/advanced_simulation_infrastructure.md}{\uline{Dominium Advanced Simulation and Infrastructure Architecture}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/app_runtime_platform_renderers.md}{\uline{Dominium APP0 Runtime, Platform, and Renderer Architecture}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/app_testx_codehygiene.md}{\uline{Dominium Architecture, Application Layer, TestX, and CodeHygiene Planning}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/architecture_codex_prompts.md}{\uline{Dominium/Domino Architecture and Codex Prompt Roadmap}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/architecture_ui_providers.md}{\uline{Dominium Architecture, UI, Providers, and Robot OS Strategy}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/build_and_future_proofing.md}{\uline{Dominium Build and Future-Proofing Architecture}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/canonical_structure_and_framework.md}{\uline{Dominium Canonical Architecture, Repository Foundation, and Provider Model}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/development_routes.md}{\uline{Dominium Development Routes and Continuity Preservation}}.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{14. Content, Packs, Modding, Providers}

The corpus repeatedly returns to pack-\allowbreak{}driven composition, authored content, providers, binary/\allowbreak{}content boundaries, and modding.\allowbreak{} Canon requires pack-\allowbreak{}driven integration and explicit refusal for missing packs.\allowbreak{} Current queue blocks package runtime and provider runtime, so promotion must be careful.\allowbreak{}


Representative sources: \href{../_reader/by_chat/advanced_simulation_infrastructure.md}{\uline{Dominium Advanced Simulation and Infrastructure Architecture}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/app_runtime_platform_renderers.md}{\uline{Dominium APP0 Runtime, Platform, and Renderer Architecture}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/app_testx_codehygiene.md}{\uline{Dominium Architecture, Application Layer, TestX, and CodeHygiene Planning}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/architecture_codex_prompts.md}{\uline{Dominium/Domino Architecture and Codex Prompt Roadmap}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/architecture_ui_providers.md}{\uline{Dominium Architecture, UI, Providers, and Robot OS Strategy}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/build_and_future_proofing.md}{\uline{Dominium Build and Future-Proofing Architecture}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/canonical_structure_and_framework.md}{\uline{Dominium Canonical Architecture, Repository Foundation, and Provider Model}}, \href{../_reader/by_chat/chronology_celestial_systems.md}{\uline{Dominium Chronology \& Celestial Systems}}.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{15. What Was Decided Across Conversations}

The strongest recurring conversation-\allowbreak{}level decisions are advisory: keep simulation truth deterministic, separate rendering from authority, keep Workbench a projection/\allowbreak{}inspection/\allowbreak{}control surface rather than truth owner, preserve source provenance, and avoid direct promotion from old chats.\allowbreak{} These are valuable because they align with current repo doctrine, but alignment is not the same as promotion.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{16. What Is Still Unresolved}

\begin{itemize}
\item Promotion candidate triage: The raw promotion queue contains useful leads but also preservation-\allowbreak{}process noise.\allowbreak{} Source: \href{../_promotion/PROMOTION_QUEUE.md}{\uline{../\_promotion/PROMOTION\_QUEUE.md}}.\allowbreak{}
\item Workbench scope: Old conversations discuss Workbench as rich operator surface, but the current queue blocks broad Workbench UI.\allowbreak{} Source: \href{../_wiki/topics/workbench.md}{\uline{../\_wiki/topics/workbench.md}}.\allowbreak{}
\item Renderer and platform boundary: Conversations repeatedly discuss renderer/\allowbreak{}platform plans, while current authority keeps rendering presentational and implementation scope blocked.\allowbreak{} Source: \href{../_wiki/topics/platform.md}{\uline{../\_wiki/topics/platform.md}}.\allowbreak{}
\item Provider and content boundaries: Provider, pack, and content discussions need separation from runtime module loading and package runtime blocks.\allowbreak{} Source: \href{../_wiki/topics/content.md}{\uline{../\_wiki/topics/content.md}}.\allowbreak{}
\item World scale and fidelity roadmap: Universe, world, chronology, and simulation conversations need sequencing against current contracts and queue limits.\allowbreak{} Source: \href{../_wiki/topics/worldgen.md}{\uline{../\_wiki/topics/worldgen.md}}.\allowbreak{}
\item Release/\allowbreak{}publication meaning: Release/\allowbreak{}versioning conversations should remain planning until release publication authority opens.\allowbreak{} Source: \href{../_wiki/topics/release.md}{\uline{../\_wiki/topics/release.md}}.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{17. Contradictions And Drift}

The audit layer contains review triggers, not resolved contradictions.\allowbreak{} The main risk classes are conversation claims against current queue restrictions, stale external/\allowbreak{}platform claims, old docs/\allowbreak{}baseline drift, and conversation-\allowbreak{}vs-\allowbreak{}conversation disagreements.\allowbreak{}


\begin{itemize}
\item \texttt{conversation\_\allowbreak{}vs\_\allowbreak{}conversation}: \texttt{2} findings.\allowbreak{}
\item \texttt{conversation\_\allowbreak{}vs\_\allowbreak{}current\_\allowbreak{}queue}: \texttt{102} findings.\allowbreak{}
\item \texttt{conversation\_\allowbreak{}vs\_\allowbreak{}docs}: \texttt{2} findings.\allowbreak{}
\item \texttt{stale\_\allowbreak{}external\_\allowbreak{}claim}: \texttt{121} findings.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\subsubsection{18. Stale Claims And Verification Queue}

External platform, SDK, renderer, language baseline, release, provider, package runtime, and implementation claims must be rechecked.\allowbreak{} The synthesis should use those old claims to identify questions, not to assert current facts.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{19. Promotion Candidates}

The raw queue contains \texttt{135} generated candidates in \href{../_promotion/PROMOTION_QUEUE.md}{\uline{PROMOTION\_QUEUE.md}}.\allowbreak{} Acceptance review found the queue useful but noisy.\allowbreak{} It should be triaged before any candidate patch work.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{20. Recommended Reconciliation Roadmap}

\begin{enumerate}
\item Keep this synthesis advisory and archive-\allowbreak{}scoped.\allowbreak{}
\item Build a claim review matrix against canon, glossary, AGENTS, current queue, contracts, schema law, and targeted current docs.\allowbreak{}
\item Triage promotion candidates into serious, historical, stale, noisy, rejected, and needs-\allowbreak{}user-\allowbreak{}decision groups.\allowbreak{}
\item Patch live docs only through narrow promotion tasks with named source claims and validation.\allowbreak{}
\end{enumerate}

\subsubsection{21. Appendices}

Current repo truth, as used by this synthesis:


\begin{itemize}
\item \href{../../../../README.md}{\uline{README.md}} describes Dominium as a deterministic, contract-\allowbreak{}governed simulation game and operating environment built on the Domino deterministic substrate.\allowbreak{}
\item \href{../../../canon/constitution_v1.md}{\uline{docs/canon/constitution\_v1.md}} binds determinism, process-\allowbreak{}only mutation, law-\allowbreak{}gated authority, no runtime mode flags, pack-\allowbreak{}driven integration, explicit refusal, and truth/\allowbreak{}perceived/\allowbreak{}render separation.\allowbreak{}
\item \href{../../../canon/glossary_v1.md}{\uline{docs/canon/glossary\_v1.md}} defines vocabulary such as Engine, Client, AuthorityContext, Domain, Derived artifact, and Contract.\allowbreak{}
\item \href{../../../../AGENTS.md}{\uline{AGENTS.md}} and \href{../../../planning/AUTHORITY_ORDER.md}{\uline{docs/planning/AUTHORITY\_ORDER.md}} keep archived conversations below canon, glossary, governance, contracts, current queue, and validated repo artifacts.\allowbreak{}
\item \href{../../../../.aide/queue/current.toml}{\uline{.aide/queue/current.toml}} currently blocks broad feature work including: \texttt{broad\_\allowbreak{}workbench\_\allowbreak{}ui}, \texttt{gameplay}, \texttt{native\_\allowbreak{}gui}, \texttt{package\_\allowbreak{}runtime}, \texttt{provider\_\allowbreak{}runtime}, \texttt{release\_\allowbreak{}publication}, \texttt{renderer\_\allowbreak{}implementation}, \texttt{runtime\_\allowbreak{}module\_\allowbreak{}loader}.\allowbreak{}
\end{itemize}

\section{Full Project Picture V0}

\vonecallout{DomSlate}{Source}{\texttt{advisory} \texttt{human\_\allowbreak{}full\_\allowbreak{}text} \texttt{derived\_\allowbreak{}synthesis} Source: \texttt{docs/\allowbreak{}archive/\allowbreak{}conversations/\allowbreak{}\_\allowbreak{}synthesis/\allowbreak{}FULL\_\allowbreak{}PROJECT\_\allowbreak{}PICTURE\_\allowbreak{}v0.\allowbreak{}md}.\allowbreak{} Reason: derived synthesis/\allowbreak{}report used as readable source.\allowbreak{}}

Source Class: conversation\_\allowbreak{}corpus\_\allowbreak{}synthesis



\subsection{Full Project Picture v0}

This map combines current repo orientation with conversation-\allowbreak{}derived design intent.\allowbreak{} When they differ, current repo authority wins.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{Product Identity}

Domino is the deterministic substrate.\allowbreak{} Dominium is the official game, product, and domain layer.\allowbreak{} Workbench is a governed validation and inspection environment.\allowbreak{} Setup and launcher compose product instances.\allowbreak{} Tools validate, generate, audit, and migrate.\allowbreak{} Contracts and schema law define public identity and compatibility meaning.\allowbreak{}


\subsubsection{Boundary Map}

\begin{center}
{\small\renewcommand{\arraystretch}{1.18}
\begin{tabularx}{\linewidth}{@{}>{\raggedright\arraybackslash}X >{\raggedright\arraybackslash}X >{\raggedright\arraybackslash}X >{\raggedright\arraybackslash}X@{}}
\toprule
\textbf{Surface} & \textbf{Current Role} & \textbf{Conversation-\allowbreak{}Derived Intent} & \textbf{Current Caution} \\
\midrule
Engine /\allowbreak{} Domino & Deterministic substrate & Reusable law-\allowbreak{}bound simulation foundation & Do not collapse into product UI \\
Game /\allowbreak{} Dominium & Domain rules and official product meaning & Invention, logistics, institutions, world systems & Gameplay remains blocked by current queue \\
Client /\allowbreak{} Renderer & Presentation and intent issuing & Rich visualization and projection & Renderer implementation is blocked \\
Server & Authoritative multiplayer validation & Law and authority keeper & Must preserve deterministic proof \\
Workbench & Validation and inspection surface & Rich operator and authoring future & Broad Workbench UI is blocked \\
Setup /\allowbreak{} Launcher & Product composition and local orchestration & Install, repair, profiles, instances & Runtime package behavior remains constrained \\
Content /\allowbreak{} Packs & Authored payload and pack-\allowbreak{}driven composition & Mods, providers, data-\allowbreak{}driven expansion & Provider/\allowbreak{}package runtime blocked \\
AIDE /\allowbreak{} Codex /\allowbreak{} XStack & Repo-\allowbreak{}control and patch workflow aids & Evidence-\allowbreak{}producing governance layer & No authority replacement \\
\bottomrule
\end{tabularx}
}
\end{center}

\subsubsection{Topic Map}

\begin{itemize}

\subsubsection{PROMOTE-0032 - architecturedoccandidate}

\begin{itemize}
